      Catudvāramidaṃ nagaraṃ āyasaṃ    pākāraṃ  
 Oruddha pati  ruddhosmiṃ kiṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā  
  
      Sabbe apihitā dvārā oruddhosmiṃ yathā dvijo    
 Kimādhikaraṇaṃ    yakkha cakkāhinihato ahaṃ  
  
      Laddhā satasahassāni atirekāni visati  
 Anukampakānaṃ ñātinaṃ vacanaṃ samma nākari  
  
      Laṅghiṃ samuddaṃ pakkhandi sāgaraṃ appasiddhikaṃ  
 Catubbhi    aṭṭhajjhagamā aṭṭhāhipi soḷasa  
 Soḷasāhi ca khattiṃsā    atricchaṃ    cakkamāsado  
 Icchāhatassa posassa cakkaṃ bhamati matthake  
  
      Upari visālā duppurā icchā visaṭagāmini  
 Ye ca taṃ anugijhanti te honti cakkadhārino  
  
      Bahuṃ bhaṇḍaṃ    apahāya    maggaṃ appaṭivekkhiya  
 Yesaṃ cetaṃ asaṅkhātaṃ     te honti cakkadhārino  
  
                  
      Kammaṃ samekkhe vipulañca bhogaṃ 
 Icchā naṃ seveyya     anatthasaṃhitaṃ  
 Kareyya vākyaṃ anukampakānaṃ 
 Taṃ tādisaṃ nātivatteyya cakkaṃ  
  
                  
      Kiva     ciraṃ nu me yakkha cakkaṃ sirasi ṭhassati  
 Kati vassasahassāni taṃ tādisaṃ nātivatteyya cakkaṃ  
  
      Atisāro accasaro mittavinda suṇohi me  
 Cakkaṃ te siramāviddhaṃ na taṃ jīvaṃ pamokkhasīti  
   Catudvārajātakaṃ  
  
                  
      Kaṇhovatāyaṃ puriso kaṇhaṃ bhuñjati bhojanaṃ  
 Kaṇhovatāyaṃ bhumippadesasmiṃ mayhaṃ mananaso piyo  
   Āsayaṃ   machasaṃ   Paṭi   machasaṃ syā   Dijo   machasaṃ syā   Kimadhi   machasaṃ 
   Catūhi   a   Dvattiṃsa   machasaṃ 
   Atricchaṃ   machasaṃ   Bahukhaṇḍaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Avahāya   machasaṃ cimu    
 Asaṅkhakhātā   machasaṃ    Seve   machasaṃ    Kiṃva   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Na kaṇho tacasā hoti antosāro brāhmaṇo 
 Yasmiṃ pāpāni kammāni sace kaṇho sujampati  
  
                   
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite  
 Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Sunikkodhaṃ    suniddosaṃ nillobhaṃ vuttimattano  
 Nisnehamabhikaṅkhāmi ete me caturo vare  
  
      Ninnu kodhe ca dose vā lobhe senaheva brāhmaṇa  
 Ādinavaṃ sampassi    taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  
  
                   
      Appo hutvā bahu hoti vaḍḍhate so akhantijo  
 Āsaṅgi bahupāyāso tasmā kodhaṃ na rocaye  
  
      Duṭṭhassa pharusā vācā parāmāso anantarā  
 Tato pāṇi tato daṇḍo satthassa paramā gati     
 Dosā kodhasamuṭṭhāno tasmā dosaṃ na rocaye  
  
      Alopasahasākārā nikati vañcanāni ca  
 Dissanti lobhadhammesu tasmā lobhaṃ na rocaye  
  
      Senaha saṅgathitā ganthā    senti manomayā puthu  
 Te bhusaṃ upatāpenti tasmā snehaṃ na rocaye  
  
                   
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite  
 Varaṃ brāhmaṇa te dammi yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi  
  
                   
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Araññe me viharato nicaṃ ekavihārino  
 Ābādhā mā uppajjeyyuṃ antarāyakarā bhusā  
  
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subāsite  
 Varaṃ brahmaṇa te dammi yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi  
  
                   
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakaka sabbabhūtānamissara 
 Na mano vā sariraṃ vā maṅkate sakka kassaci 
 Kadāvi apahaññetha etaṃ sakka varaṃ vareti  
   Kaṇhajātakaṃ  
  
   Sunikodhaṃ   machasaṃ   Ādinavaṃ sampassi   machasaṃ   Parāmasati   machasaṃ syā 
   Saṅgatthitā   syā  
  
                    
      Yo kopaneyye na karoti kopaṃ  
 Na kujjhati sappuriso kadāci  
 Kuddhopi yo nāvikarāti loke  
 Taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
      Ūnodaro    yo sahate jighacchaṃ 
 Danto tapassi    mitapānabhojano  
 Āhārahetu na kāroti pāpaṃ 
 Taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
      Khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ vippajahitva    sabbaṃ 
 Na cālikaṃ bhāsati kiñci loke  
 Vibhusanaṭṭhānā virato methunasmā 
 Taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
      Pariggahaṃ lohadhammañca sabbaṃ 
 Yo ce pariññāya paribbajeti  
 Dantaṃ ṭhitattaṃ amamaṃ nirāsaṃ 
 Taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
      Pucchāma kattāraṃ anomapaññaṃ 
 Gāthāsu no viggaho atthi jato  
 Chindajja kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni 
 Tayajja kaṅkhaṃ vitaremu sabbe  
  
      Ye paṇḍitā atthadassā bhavanti 
 Bhāsanti te yoniso tattha kāle  
 Kathaṃ nu gāthānaṃ    abhāsitānaṃ atthaṃ nayeyyuṃ kusalā janinda  
  
      Kathaṃ bhave bhāsati nāgarājā 
 Kathaṃ pana garuḷo venateyyo    
 Gandhabbarājā pana kiṃ vadeti 
 Kathaṃ pana kurunaṃ rājaseṭṭho  
  
      Khantiṃ bhatva bhāsati nāgarājā 
 Appahāraṃ garuḷo venateyyo gandhabbarājā rativippahānaṃ 
 Akiñcanaṃ kurunaṃ rājaseṭṭhāti   
  
      Sabbāni etāni subhāsitāni 
 Nahettha dubbhāsitamatthi kiñci  
 Yasmiñca etāni patiṭṭhitāni 
 Arāva nābhyā    susamohitāni  
 Catubbhi dhammehi samaṅgibhūtaṃ 
 Taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
   Samaṇamāhu   machasaṃ syā   Onodaro   syā   Tapisaṃ   machasaṃ   Vippajahitvāna 
   machasaṃ syā   Kathānaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Garuḷo pana venateyye kimāha   machasaṃ 
 syā   Nabhyā   machasaṃ syā   ayaṃ gāthā muddita jātakapāḷiyaṃ natthi  
  
                    
  
      Tuvaṃ    seṭṭho tvamanuttarosi 
 Tvaṃ dhammagu dhammavidu sumedho 
 Paññāya pañhaṃ samadhiggahetvā  
 Acchecchi dhīro vicikicchitāni 
 Acchecchi    kaṅkhaṃ vivikicchitāni 
 Cundo yathā nāgadantaṃ kharena  
  
      Niluppalāhaṃ vimalaṃ anāgaghaṃ 
 Vatthaṃ imaṃ    dhumasamānavaṇṇaṃ  
 Pañcassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho 
 Dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhīra  
  
      Suṇṇamālaṃ satapattathulalaṃ    
 Sakesaraṃ ratanasabhassamaṇaḍitaṃ 
 Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho 
 Dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhīra  
      Maṇiṃ anagghaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ  
 Kaṇṭhāvasattaṃ maṇibhusitaṃ me  
 Pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho 
 Dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhīra  
  
      Gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ  
 Ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime  
 Pañahassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho 
 Dadāmi te gāmavarāni soḷasāti  
   Catuposathikajātakaṃ   
  
                   
      Bahussuto sutadhammosi saṅkha 
 Diṭṭhā tayā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca  
 Athakkhaṇe dassayase vilāpaṃ 
 Aññonu ko te paṭimantako mayā  
  
                   
      Subbhu subhā suppaṭimuttakambu 
 Paggayha sovaṇṇamayāya    pātiyā    
 Bhuñajassu bhattaṃ iti maṃ vadeti 
 Saddhā    cittā tamhaṃ noti brūmi  
  
   Tuvaṃ hi   machasaṃ syā   Acchejji   machasaṃ syā  
   Phullikaṃ   machasaṃ syā   vidhurajātake   puṇṇakajātaketipi vadanti   Sovaṇṇamayā 
   machasaṃ   Pāṭiyā   syā   Tadā   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Etādisaṃ brāhmaṇa disva    yakkhaṃ 
 Succheyya poso sukhamāsasāno    
 Uṭṭhehi taṃ pañajalikāhi puccha    
 Devinusi tvaṃ uda mānusī nu  
  
                   
      Yaṃ tvaṃ sukhenābhisamekkhase maṃ 
 Bhuñajassu bhattaṃ iti maṃ vadesi  
 Pucchāmi taṃ nāri mahānubhave    
 Devinusi tvaṃ uda mānusi nu  
  
      Devi ahaṃ saṅkha mahānubhāvā 
 Idhāgatā sāgaravārimajjhe  
 Anukampikā no ca paduṭṭhacittā 
 Tameva atthāya idhāgatosmi  
  
      Idhannapānaṃ sayanāsanañca 
 Yānāni nānā vividhāni saṅkha  
 Sabbassa tyāhaṃ paṭipādayāmi 
 Yaṃ kiñci tuyhaṃ manasābhipatthitaṃ  
  
      Yaṃ kiñci yiṭṭhaṃva hutaṃ va mayhaṃ 
 Sabbassa no issarā tvaṃ sugatte  
 Sussoṇi subbhu suvilākamajjhe 
 Kissa me kammassa ayaṃ vipāko  
  
                   
      Ghamme pathe brāhmaṇa ekabhikkhuṃ 
 Ugghaṭṭapādaṃ tasitaṃ kilantaṃ  
 Paṭipādayi saṅkha upāhanāhi 
 Sā dakkhiṇā kāmaduhā tavajja  
  
      Sā hotu nāvā phalakuppantā 
 Anavassutā erakavātayuttā  
 Aññassa yānassa na hettha bhumi 
 Ajjeva maṃ molinaṃ pāpayassu  
  
                   
      Sā tattha cittā    sumanā patitā 
 Nāvaṃ sucittaṃ abhinimmiṇitvā  
 Ādāya saṅkhaṃ purisena saddhiṃ 
 Upānayi nagaraṃ sādhu rammanti  
   Saṅkhajātakaṃ  
  
   Disvāna vi   machasaṃ syā   Māsasamāno   machasaṃ māsisāno   si 
   Pucchā   machasaṃ   Mahānubhāvena   machasaṃ   Tuṭṭhavittā   machasaṃ syā  
  
                   
                    
      Yo te imaṃ visālakkhi piyaṃ sammillabhāsiniṃ    
 Ādāya balā gaccheyya kinnu kayirāsi brāhmaṇa  
  
      Uppajja    me na mucceyya na me mucceyya  jivato 
 Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi khippameva nivāraye  
  
                   
      Yannu pubbe vikatthittho    balamhi ca apassito  
 Svājja    tuṇhikakodāni    saṅghāṭiṃ sibbamacchasi  
  
      Uppajja me na mucceyya na me mucceyya jivato 
 Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi khippameva nivārayi  
  
      Kinne uppajji no mucci    kinne no mucci jivato  
 Rajaṃva vipulā vuṭṭhi katamaṃ tvaṃ nivārayī  
  
                   
      Yamhi jāte na passati ajāte sādhu passati  
 So me uppajjati no mucci kodho dummedhagocaro  
  
      Yena jātena nandanti amittā dukkhamesino  
 So me uppajjati no mucci kodho dummedhagocaro  
      Yasmiñca jayamānasmiṃ sadatthaṃ nāvakhujjhati   
 So me uppajjati no mucci kodho dummedhagocaro  
      Yenāhibhuto kusalaṃ jahāti 
 Parakkare vipulañcāpi atthaṃ  
 Sa bhimaseno balavā pamaddi 
 Kodho mahārāja na me amuccatha  
  
      Kaṭṭhasmiṃ manthamānasmiṃ pāvako nāma jāyati  
 Tameva kaṭṭhaṃ ḍahati yasmā so jāyate gini  
  
   Samahita bhāsiniṃ   machasaṃ saṃsilabhāsani   syā   Uppajje rā uppajji   machasaṃ syā 
   Muñceyya   machasaṃ syā 
   Vikatthito   machasaṃ syā   Svajja   machasaṃ 
   Tuṇhitato   machasaṃ   Muñcittha   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
      Evaṃ mandassa posassa bālassa avijānato 
 Sārambhā jāyate kodho sopi teneva ḍahayhati    
  
      Aggiva tiṇakaṭṭhasmiṃ kodho pavaḍḍhati  
 Nihiyati tassa yaso kāḷapakkheva candimā  
  
      Anindho    dhumaketuva kodho yassupasammati  
 Āpurati tassa yaso sukkapakkheva candimāti  
   Cullabodhijātakaṃ  
  
                   
      Santāhamevāhaṃ pasannacitto 
 Puññatthiko acariṃ    brahmacariyaṃ 
 Athāparaṃ yaṃ caritaṃ mamayidaṃ    
 Vassāni paññāsa samādhikāni 
 Akāmako vāpi ahaṃ carāmi 
 Etena saccena suvatthi 
 Hataṃ visaṃ jivatu yaññadatto  
  
                   
      Yasmā dānaṃ nābhinandiṃ kadāci 
  Disvānāhaṃati atithiṃ vāsakāle  
 Nacāpi me appiyataṃ aveduṃ 
 Bahussutā samaṇā brahmanā ca    
 Akāmako vā hi ahaṃ dadāmi  
 E tena saccena savatthi hotu 
 Hataṃ visaṃ jivatu yaññadatto  
  
      Āsiviso tāta pahutatejo    
 Yo taṃ adaṃsi    khilarā    udicca tasmiñca me appiyatāya ajja  
 Pitarañca te natthi koci viseso 
 E tena saccena savatthi hotu 
 Hataṃ visaṃ jivatu yaññadatto  
  
                   
      Santā dantā yeva paribbajanti 
 Aññatra kaṇhā anakāmarūpā  
 Dipāyana kissa jigucchamāno 
 Akāmako carasi brahmacariyaṃ  
  
   Dahati   machasaṃ syā dayhati   machasaṃ syā   Aniḍo   machasaṃ syā 
   Ācari   machasaṃ syā   Mamedaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Samaṇabrāhmaṇa   machasaṃ   Bahutta   machasaṃ 
   Adhasi   syā adasi   machasaṃ   Khilārā   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Saddhāya nikkhamma punaṃ    nivatto 
 So eḷamugova balo   vatāyaṃ  
 Etassa vādassa jigucchamano 
 Akāmako carāmi brahmacariyaṃ 
 Viññappasatthañca    satañca ṭhānaṃ 
 Evampahaṃ puññakāro bhavāmi  
  
                   
      Samaṇe tuvaṃ brāhmaṇe addhike ca 
 Santappayāsi antapānena bhikkhaṃ  
 Opānabhūtaṃ ca gharaṃ tavayidaṃ 
 Annena pānena upetarūpaṃ 
 Atha kissa vādassa jigucchamano 
 Akāmako dānamimaṃ dadāsi  
  
      Pitaro ca me āsuṃ pitāmahā ca 
 Saddhā ahu   dānapati vadañña 
 Taṃ kullavantaṃ    anuvattamāno  
 Māhaṃ kule antima gandhino ahuṃ etassa vādassa jigucchamano 
 Akāmako dānamimaṃ dadāsi  
  
                   
      Dahariṃ kumāriṃ asamatthapaññaṃ 
 Yaṃ tānayiṃ    ñātikulā sugatte 
 Na cāpi me appiyataṃ avedi  
 Aññatra kāmā paricārayanti    
 Atha kena vaṇṇena mayā te    hoti 
 Saṃvāsadhammo ahu evarūpo  
  
      Ārā dūre na idha    kadāci atthi 
 Paramparā nāma kule imasmiṃ 
 Taṃ kullavantaṃ anuvattamānā  
 Māhaṃ kule antimagandhini ahuṃ 
 Etassa vādasasa jigucchamānā 
 Akāmikā     baddhacarāsmi tuyhaṃ  
  
                   
      Maṇḍavya bhāsissaṃ abhāsaneyyaṃ     
 Taṃ khamyataṃ puttahetu mamajja  
 Puttapemā     na idha paratthi kiñci  
 So no ayaṃ jīvati yaññadattoti  
   Kaṇhadīpāyanajātakaṃ  
  
   Puna   machasaṃ syā   Parivārayantā   machasaṃ syā 
   Capalo   machasaṃ syā   Hi   machasaṃ syā 
   Viññupasaṭṭhaṃ   machasaṃ   Hi   machasaṃ  
   Ahuṃ   machasaṃ    Akāmakā   machasaṃ 
   Kulavattaṃ   machasaṃ syā    Bhāsiṃ samabhāsamaneyaṃ   machasaṃ   Ānayi   
 machasaṃ    Taṃ puttapemaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                   
                    
      Nacāhametaṃ jānāmi kovāyaṃ kassa cāti vā    
 Yathā sākho vadi evaṃ nigrodha kinti maññasi  
  
      Tato galavinitena purisā nihariṃsu maṃ  
 Datvā mukha pahārāni sākhassa vacanaṃ karā  
  
      Etādisaṃ dummatinā akataññuta    dubbhinā  
 Kataṃ anariyaṃ sākhena sākhinā te janādhipa  
  
                   
      Ncāhaṃ metaṃ jānāmi napi me koci saṃsati  
 Yamme tvaṃ samma akkhāsi sakhena kaḍḍhanaṃ kataṃ    
  
      Sakhīnaṃ sājivakāro mama sākhassa cubhayaṃ  
 Tvaṃ no issariyaṃ dātā manusessu mahaggataṃ  
 Tayambhā labhitā iddhi ettha me natthi saṃsayo  
  
      Yathāpi khijaṃ aggismiṃ ḍayhati na viruhati  
 Evaṃ kataṃ asappurise nassati na virūhati  
  
      Kataññumhī ca posambhi sīlavante ariyavuttine  
 Sukhette viya khijāni kataṃ kambhi na nassati  
  
      Imañca jammaṃ    nekatikaṃ asappurisacintakaṃ    
 Hanattu sākhaṃ satthihi nāssa icchāmi jīvitaṃ  
  
                   
      Khamyatassa    mahārāja pāṇā duppaṭiānayā  
 Khama dve asappurisassa nāssa icchāmahaṃ vadhaṃ  
  
      Nigrodhameva seveyya na sākhamupasaṃvase  
 Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo yañce sākhasmiṃ jīvitanti  
   Nigrodhajātakaṃ  
  
   Cāti vā   machasaṃ   Akatañakadunā   machasaṃ akataññena   syā 
   Karaṇaṃ machasaṃ   Imaṃ   machasaṃ   Cittitaṃ   machasaṃ   Khamitassa   machasaṃ 
 syā 
  
                   
                    
      Na takkaḷā santi na ālupāni 
 Na khiḷāliyo na kalambāni tāta eko araññambhi susānamajjhe 
 Kimatthiko tāta khaṇāsi    kāsuṃ  
  
      Pitāmaho tāta sudubbalo te 
 Anekavyādhihi dukhena    phuṭṭho  
 Tamajjahaṃ nikhaṇissāmi sobbhe 
 Nahissa taṃ jīvitaṃ rocayāmi 
  
      Saṅkappametaṃ paṭiladdha pāpaṃ 
 Accāhitaṃ kamma karosi luddaṃ  
                   
 Mayāpi tāta paṭilacchase tuvaṃ 
 Etādisaṃ kamma    jarūpanito    
 Taṃ kullavantaṃ anuvattamāno 
 Ahampi taṃ nikhaṇissāmi sobbhe  
  
      Pharusāhi vācāhi pakubbamāne 
 Āsajja maṃ tvaṃ vadase kumāra  
 Putto mama orasako samāno 
 Abhitānukampi me tvaṃsi putta  
  
      Na tāhaṃ    tāta abhitānukampi  
 Hitānukampi te ahaṃpi tāta  
 Pāpañca taṃ kamma pakubbamānaṃ 
 Arahāmi no vārayituṃ tato hi  
  
      Yo mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā vasiṭṭha    
 Adusake hiṃsati pāpadhammo  
 Kāyassa bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ 
 Asaṃsayaṃ so sugatiṃ pareti  
  
                   
      Yo mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā vasiṭṭha 
 Annena pānena upaṭṭhahāti  
 Kāyassa bhedā abhisamparāyaṃ 
 Asaṃsayaṃ so sugatiṃ pareti  
  
      Na me tvaṃ putta abhitānukampi 
 Hitānukampi me tvaṃ si putta  
 Ahañca taṃ mātarā vuccamāno 
 Etādisaṃ kamma karomi ludadaṃ  
  
   Khaṇasi   machasaṃ   Dukkhena   machasaṃ syā   Kammaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Jaropanito  machasaṃ   Tyāhaṃ   machasaṃ   Saviṭṭha   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
  
      Yā te sā bhariyā anariyarūpā  
 Matā mamesā sakiyā    janenti 
 Niddhāpayetaṃ sakā agārā 
 Aññampi te sā dukha    māvaheyya  
  
                   
      Yā te sā bhariyā anariyarūpā  
 Matā mamesā sakiyā janenti 
 Dannā kareṇuva vasupanitā 
 Sā pāpadhammā punarāvajātuti   Takkalajātakaṃ  
  
                   
      Kinne vataṃ kimpana brahmacariyaṃ 
 Kissa suciṇṇassa ayaṃ vipāko  
 Akkhāhi me brāhmaṇa etamatthaṃ 
 Kasmā hi tumbhaṃ daharā na miyare  
  
                   
      Dhammaṃ carāma na musā bhaṇāma 
 Pāpāni kammāni vivajjayāma  
 Anariyaṃ parivajjemu sabbaṃ 
 Ta smā hi ambhaṃ daharā na mīyare  
  
      Suṇoma dhammaṃ asataṃ sataṃ ca 
 Na cāpi dhammaṃ asataṃ rocayāma 
 Hitvā asante na jahāma sante 
 Ta smā hi ambhaṃ daharā na mīyare 
  
      Subbeva dānā sumanā bhavāma 
 Dadampi ce antamanā bhavāma  
 Datvāpi ce nānutappāma    pacchā ta smā hi ambhaṃ daharā na mīyare  
  
      Samaṇe mayaṃ brāhmaṇe addhike ca 
 Vaṇibbake sācanake daḷidde  
 Annena pānena abhitappayāma   ta smā hi ambhaṃ daharā na mīyare  
   Jātiyā   machasaṃ   Dukkha   simu   Nānu tapāma   machasaṃ   Abhitapāma   
 machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Mayañca bhariyā nātikkamāma 
 Ambhe ca bhariyā nātikkamanti  
 Aññatu tāhi brahmacariyaṃ carāma 
 Tasmā hi ambhaṃ daharā na mīyare  
  
      Pāṇātipāti viramāma sabbe 
 Loke adidantaṃ parivajjayāma  
 Amajjapā no ca musā bhaṇāma 
 Tasmā hi ambhaṃ daharā na miyare  
  
      Etāsu ce jāyare suttamāsu 
 Medhāvino honti pahutapaññā    
 Bahussutā vedaguno ca    honti 
 Tasmā hi ambhaṃ daharā na miyare  
  
      Etāsu ce jāyare suttamāsu  
 Medhāvino honti pahutapaññā     
 Bahussutā vedaguno ca    honti 
 Tasmā hi ambhaṃ daharā na miyare  
  
      Mātāpitā ca bhagini bhātaro ca 
 Puttā ca dārā ca mayañca sabbe  
 Dhammaṃ carāma paralokahetu  
 Tasmā hi ambhaṃ daharā na miyare  
                   
      Dāsā ca dasso    anujivino ca 
 Paricārakā kammakarā ca sabbe  
 Dhammaṃ caranti paralokahetu  
 Tasmā hi ambhaṃ daharā na miyare  
  
      Dhammo bhave rakkhati dhammacāriṃ 
 Dhammo suciṇṇo sukhamāvahāti 
 Esānisaṃso dhammo suciṇeṇa 
 Na duggatiṃ gacchati dhammacārī  
  
                   
      Dhammo bhave rakkhati dhammacāriṃ 
 Chattaṃ mahantaṃ viya vassakāle  
 Dhammena gutto mama dhammapālo  
 Aññassa aṭṭhiti sukhī kumāroti  
   Mahādhammapālajātakaṃ  
  
   Pahutta   machasaṃ bahuta   syā   Vedaguṇā   machasaṃ   Dāso  machasaṃ dāsi   syā 
  
                   
                    
      Nāsmase katapāpambhi nāsmase alikavādine nāsmasantaṭṭhapaññambhi    atisantepi 
    nāsamase  
  
      Bhavanti heke purisā gopipāsakajātikā  
 Ghasanti maññe mittāni vācāya na ca kammunā  
  
      Sukkhañajali paggahitā vācāya paḷiguṇṭhitā 
 Sakuddapheggu nāside yasmiṃ natthi kataññutā  
  
                   
      Na hi aññañña    cittānaṃ itthīnaṃ purisāna    vā  
 Nānāva katvā saṃsaggaṃ tādisampi nāsamase  
  
      Anariyakammaṃ okkantaṃ    atthetaṃ    sabba ghātinaṃ    
 Nisitaṃva paṭicchannaṃ tādisampi nāsmase  
  
      Vittarūpenidhekacce sākhallena    acetasā  
 Vividhehi upāyehi    tāsisampi nāsamase  
  
      Āmisaṃ vā dhanaṃ vāpi yattha passati tādiso  
 Dubhiṃ     karoti dummedho tañca jhatavāna     gacchati  
  
                   
      Mittarūpena bahavo chantā sevanti sattavo  
 Jahe kāpurisehete kukkuṭo viya senakaṃ  
  
      Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ na khippamanuṇujjhati  
 Amittavasamanovati pacchā ca manutappati  
  
      Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ khippameva nibodhati  
 Muccate satatusambādhā kukkuṭo viya senakā  
      Taṃ tādisaṃ kuṭamivoḍḍitaṃ     vane 
 Adhammikaṃ niccavidhaṃsakārinaṃ  
 Ārā vivajjeyya nāro vicakkhaṇo 
 Senaṃ yathā kukkuṭo vaṃsakānaneti  
    Kukkuṭajātakaṃ  
  
   Nāsmase attatatha paññambhi   syā   Attasantepi   machasaṃ 
   Aññoñña   syā   Aññoñña   syā 
   Purisanaṃ   machasaṃ   Mukakantaṃ   syā 
   Athetaṃ   machasaṃ   Ghāṭinaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Sābbalena   machasaṃ syā   Upāyanti   machasaṃ syā 
    Dubbhiṃ   machasaṃ syā    Hanatvāna   machasaṃ syā 
    Kuṭṭa   machasaṃ 
  
                   
                    
      Alaṅkato maṭṭakuṇḍali  
 Mālāhāri haricandanussado  
 Bāhā paggayha nandasi 
 Vanamajjhe kiṃ dukkhito tuvaṃ  
  
      Sovaṇṇamayo pahassaro 
 Uppanno athapañajaro mama 
 Tassa cakkayugaṃ na vindāmi 
 Tena dukkhena jahāmi jititaṃ  
  
      Sovaṇṇamayaṃ maṇimayaṃ 
 Lohamayaṃ atha rūpiyāmayaṃ  
 Pāvada rathaṃ kārayāmi te 
 Cakkayugaṃ paṭipādayāmi taṃ  
  
      So māṇavo tassa pāvadi 
 Candasuriyā ubhayettha bhātaro sovaṇṇamayo raratho mama 
 Tena cakkayugena sobhati  
  
                   
      Bālo kho tvamasi māṇava 
 Yo tvaṃ patthayase apatthiyaṃ    
 Maññāmi tuvaṃ marissasi 
 Na hi tvaṃ    lacchasi candasuriye  
  
      Gamanāgamanampi dissati 
 Vaṇṇadhātu ubhayettha vithiyo  
 Peto pana neva dissati 
 Ko nu kho kandataṃ bālyataro  
  
      Saccaṃ kho vadesi māṇava 
 Ahameva kandataṃ bālyataro  
 Candaṃ viya dārako rudaṃ 
 Petaṃ kālakatāhipatthaye  
  
      Ādinnaṃ vata maṃ mantaṃ ghatasittaṃ va pāvakaṃ  
 Vārinā viya osiñcaṃ sabbaṃ nibbāpaye daraṃ  
                   
      Sohaṃ abbuḷhasallosmi vitasoko anāvilo  
 Na socāmi na rodāmi tava sutvāna māṇavāti  
    Maṭṭakuṇḍalijātakaṃ  
  
   Apatthayaṃ   machasaṃ   syā   Natvaṃ   machasaṃ   Abbuḷhaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Yamāsi hadayassitaṃ   machasaṃ   syā  
  
                    
                   
      Apacantāpi    dicchanti sanno laddhāna bhojanaṃ  
 Kimeva tvaṃ pacamāno yaṃ na dajjā na taṃ samaṃ  
  
      Maccherā ca pamādā ca evaṃ dānaṃ na diyati  
 Puññaṃ ākaṅkhamānena deyyaṃ hoti vijānatā  
  
      Yasseva hito na dadāti macchari tareva adadato bhayaṃ  
 Jighacchā ca pipāsā ca yassa bhāyati macchari  
 Tameva bālaṃ phusati    asmiṃ loke paramhi ca  
  
      Tasmā vineyya maccheraṃ dajjā dānaṃ malābhibhu  
 Puññāti paralokasmiṃ patiṭṭhā honti pāṇinaṃ  
  
                   
      Duddadaṃ dadamānānaṃ dukkaraṃ kamma kubbataṃ  
 Asanto nānukubbanti sataṃ dhammo durantayo  
  
      Tasmā satañca asatañca nānā hoti ito gati  
 Asanto nirayaṃ yanti santo saggaparāyanā  
  
      Appasemake pavecchinti    bahuneke    na dicchare  
 Appasmā dakkhiṇā dintā sahassena samaṃ mitā  
  
                   
      Dhammaṃ care yopi samuñajakaṃ    care dārañca  posaṃ dadaṃ appakasmiṃ  
 Sataṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ 
 Kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te  
  
      Kenesa yañño vipulo mahagghano 
 Samenana dinnassa na agghameti  
 Kathaṃ sahassānaṃ sahassa yāginaṃ 
 Kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa te  
  
                   
      Dadanti heke visame niviṭṭhā 
 Jhatvā    vadhitvā atha socayitvā  
 Sā dakkhiṇā assumukhā sadaṇḍā 
 Samena dinnassa na agghameti 
 Evaṃ sahassānaṃ sahassayāginaṃ 
 Kalampi nāgghanti tathāvidhassa teti  
    Khiḷārakosiyajātakaṃ  
  
   Apacayantopi   machasaṃ   Phusasati   machasaṃ   Appameke pavacchanti   machasaṃ 
   Bahunā eke   syā 
   Samuñajikaṃ   machasaṃ   Puttadāraṃ   machasaṃ   Jhetvā   machasaṃ  
  
                   
                    
      Vaṇṇavā abhirūposi ghano sañajātarohito  
 Cakakkavāka surūposi vippasannamukhindriyo  
  
      Pāṭhinaṃ    pāvusaṃ macchaṃ valajaṃ muñajarohitaṃ  
 Gaṅgāya tīre nisinto    evaṃ bhuñjasi bhojanaṃ  
  
                   
      Na cāhametaṃ bhuñjāmi jaṅgalā nodakāni vā  
 Aññatra sevālapaṇakā etaṃ me samma bhojanaṃ  
  
      Na cāhametaṃ saddahāmi cakkavākassa bhojanaṃ  
 Ahaṃ hi    samma bhuñjāmi gāme loṇiyateliyaṃ  
  
      Manussesu kataṃ bhattaṃ sucimaṃsupasecanaṃ  
 Na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo cakkavāka yathā tavaṃ  
  
      Sampassaṃ antani veraṃ hiṃsayaṃ    mānusiṃ pajaṃ  
 Utusto ghasasi hito tena vaṇeṇā tavediso  
  
      Sabbaloka viraddhosi    dhaṅka pāpena kammunā  
 Laddho piṇḍo na piṇeti tena vaṇena tavediso  
  
      Ahampi samma bhuñjāmi ahiṃsā    sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 Apposasukko nirāsaṅki asoko akuto bhayo  
  
      So karassu anubhāvaṃ vitivattassu siliyaṃ  
 Ahiṃsāya varaṃ loke piyo hohisi mamiva  
  
      Yo na hanti na ghāteti na jināti napāpaye  
 Mettaṃso sabbabhutesu veraṃ tassa na kenaciti  
    Cakkavātajātakaṃ  
  
   Pātinaṃ   machasaṃ   Gaṅgā tīre nisinnosi   machasaṃ syā 
   Ahaṃpi   syā   Hiṃsāya   machasaṃ syā 
   Ciruddhosi   machasaṃ   syā   Abhiṃsa   machasaṃ 
  
                   
                    
      Saccaṃ kira tvampi bhuripañño     
 Yā tādisi siri dhiti muti    ca  
 Na tāyate bhāvavasupanitaṃ 
 Yo yāvakaṃ bhuñjasi appasupaṃ  
  
      Sukhaṃ dukkhena paripācayanto 
 Kālākālaṃ vicinaṃ chandachanto    
 Atthassa dvārāni avāpuranto 
 Tenāhaṃ    tussāmi yavodanena  
  
      Kālañca ñatvā abhijihanāya 
 Mantehi atthaṃ paripācayitvā  
 Vijambhissaṃ    sihavijamhitāni 
 Tāyiddhiyā dakkhasi maṃ punāpi  
  
      Sukhihi eke    na kāronti pāpaṃ  
 Avaṇaṇasaṃsaggabhayā puneke  
 Pahu samāno vipulatthavinti 
 Kiṃ kāraṇā me na kārosi dukkhaṃ  
  
      Na paṇḍitā antasukhassa hetu 
 Pāpāni kammāni samācaranti  
 Dukkhena puṭṭhā khalitattāpi santā 
 Chandā ca dosā na jahanti dhammaṃ  
  
      Yena kenaci vaṇeṇana mudunā dāruṇena vā  
 Uddhare dinamantānaṃ pacchā dhammaṃ samācare  
  
      Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideya sayeyya vā  
 Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubbho hi pāpako  
  
      Yassāhi dhammaṃ    manujo vijaññā 
 Yecassa kaṅkhaṃ vinayanti santo  
 Taṃ hissa dipañca parāyaṇañca 
 Na tena mittaṃ jarayetha    pañño  
  
   Bhuripañña   machasaṃ   Mati   machasaṃ   Chinnachanno   machasaṃ 
   Tenāha   machasaṃ   Vichambhisaṃ   machasaṃ   Sukhī pi ete   machasaṃ 
   Yassa hi dhamma puriso vijaññā   machasaṃ   Jiyetha   syā 
  
                    
      Alaso gihi kāmabhogi na sādhu 
 Asaññato pabbajito na sādhu  
 Rājā na sādhu anisammakāri 
 Yo paṇḍito kodhano taṃ na sādhu  
  
      Nisamma khantiyo kayirā nānisamma disampati  
 Nisammakārino rāja yaso kinti ca vaḍḍhatiti  
    Bhuripaññajātakaṃ  
  
                   
      Kiṃ su naro jappamadhiccakāle 
 Kaṃ vā vijjaṃ katamaṃ vā sutānaṃ  
 So macco asamiñca parambhi loke 
 Kathaṃ karo sotthānena gutto  
  
      Yassa devā pitaro ca sabba 
 Siriṃsapā    sabbabhūtāni cāpi  
 Mettāya niccaṃ apacitāni honti 
 Bhutesu ce sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
                   
      Yo pabbalokasa nivātavutti 
 Itthi pumānaṃ saha dārakānaṃ  
 Khantā duruttānaṃ apaṭikkulavādi 
 Adhivāsanaṃ sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
      Yo nāvajānāti sahāyamatte 
 Sippena kalyāhi dhanena jaccā  
 Rucipañño atthakāle mutimā 
 Sahāyesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
      Mittāni ve yassa bhavanti santo 
 Saṃvissatthā    avisaṃvādakassa  
 Na mittaduhi    saṃvihāgi dhanena 
 Mittesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu 
  
      Yassa bhariya tulyavayā mahaggā 
 Anubbatā dhammakāmā pajātā    
 Koliniyā silavati patibbatā 
 Dāresu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
   Sarisapā   machasaṃ   Saṃvissaṭṭhā   machasaṃ   Na mitta dubbhi   machasaṃ 
   Sajātā   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Yassa rājā bhūtapati yasassi 
 Jānāti soceyyaṃ    parakkamañca  
 Advejjhatāsu    bhadayaṃ mamanti 
 Rājusu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
      Antañca pānañca dadāti saddho 
 Mālañca gandhañca vilepananañca    
 Pasantacitto anumodamāno 
 Saggesu ve sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
                   
      Yamariyadhammena punanti vaddhā    
 Ārādhitā samacariyāya santo  
 Bahussutā isayo    silavantaṃ 
 Arahantamajjhe sotthānaṃ tadāhu  
  
                   
      Etāni kho sotthānāti loke 
 Viññuppasatthāni    sukhuduyāni  
 Tānidha sevetha nāro sapañño 
 Na hi maṅgale kikañcanamatthi    saccanti  
    Mahāmaṅgalajātakaṃ  
  
                   
      Uṭṭhehi kaṇha kiṃ sesi ko attho supine tena 
 Yopi tuyha sako bhātā bhadayaṃ cakkhuñca    dakkhiṇaṃ 
 Tassa vātā baliyanti ghato jappati kesava  
  
                   
      Tassasa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā rohiṇeyyassa kesavo  
 Taramānarūpo vuṭṭhāsi bhātusokena aṭṭitā  
  
      Kinnu ummattarūpova kevalaṃ dvārakaṃ imaṃ  
 Saso sasoti lapasi ko nu te sasamāhari  
  
      Sovaṇaṇamayaṃ maṇimayaṃ lohamayaṃ atha rūpiyāmayaṃ  
 Saṅkhasilāpavāḷamayaṃ kārayissāmi te sasaṃ  
  
      Santi aññapi sasakā araññe vanagocarā  
 Tepi te ānayissāmi kidisaṃ sasamicchasi  
  
   Soveyya   machasaṃ   Amijjhatā   machasaṃ   Vibhusanañca   machasaṃ 
   Punatti vuddhā   machasaṃ   Issayo   machasaṃ   Viññadupasaṭṭhāni   machasaṃ 
   Kiṃcina   syā   Cakkhu   machasaṃ  
                    
      Nacāhametaṃ icchāmi ye sasā paṭhiviṃ sitā  
 Candato sasamicchāmi tamme obhara kesava  
  
                   
      So nūna madhuraṃ ñāti jīvitaṃ vijahissasi  
 Apatthiyaṃ yo patthayasi candato sasamicchasi  
  
      Evañce kaṇha jānāsi yadaññamanusāssi  
 Kasmā pure mataṃ puttaṃ ajjāpimanusocasi  
  
      Yaṃ na labbhā manussena amanussena vā puna    
 Jato me māmari putto kuto labbhā alabbhiyaṃ  
  
      Na mantā mulabhesajjā osadhehi dhanena vā  
 Sakkā ānayituṃ kaṇhā yampetamanusocasi  
  
                   
      Yassa etādisā assu amaccā purisapaṇḍitā  
 Yathā nijjhāpaye ajja ghato purisapaṇḍito  
  
      Ādinnaṃ vata maṃ santaṃ ghatasintaṃ va pāvakaṃ vārinā viya osiñcaṃ sabbaṃ 
 nibbāpaye daraṃ  
  
      Abbahi vata me sallaṃ yamāsi hadayanissitaṃ  
 Yo me sokaparetassa puttasokaṃ apānudi  
  
      Sohaṃ abbuḷhasallosmi vitasoko anāvilo  
 Na socāmi na rodāmi tava sutvāna māṇava  
  
      Evaṃ karonti sappaññā ye honti anukampakā  
 Nivattayanti sokamhā ghato jeṭṭhaṃva bhātaranti  
    Ghatapaṇḍitajātakaṃ  
  
 Dasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Daḷhakaṇhadhanañcayasaṅkhavaro 
 Rājā sattāha sasakha takkaḷinā  
 Dhammaṃ kukkuṭakuṇḍalibhojanadā 
 Cakkavāka subhurisasotthi ghattā 
  
   Pana   machasaṃ 
  
                   
                    
      Tassa nāgassa vippavāsena 
 Virūḷhā sallaki    ca kuṭajā ca  
 Kuruvindakaravarā bhisasāmā    
 Nivāte pupphitā ca kaṇikārā    
  
      Kovideva suvaṇaṇakāyurā  
 Nāgarājaṃ bharanti piṇḍena  
 Yattha rājā rājakumāro vā 
 Kavacambhihessati asamabhito  
  
                   
      Gaṇhāhi nāga kabaḷaṃ mā nāga kisako bhava  
 Bahuni rājakiccāni yāni    nāga karissasi  
  
      Sā nūna sā kapaṇikā andhā aparināyikā  
 Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃpati  
  
      Kā nu te sā mahānāga andhā aparināyikā  
 Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃpati  
      Mātā me sā mahārāja andhā aparināyikā  
 Khāṇuṃ pādena ghaṭṭeti giriṃ caṇḍoraṇaṃpati  
  
      Muñcathetaṃ mahānāgaṃ yo yaṃ bharati mātaraṃ  
 Sametu mātarā nāgo saha sabbehi ñātihi  
  
      Muttoca bandhanā nāgo kāsirājena pesito  
 Muhuttaṃ vissamitvāna    agamā yena pabbato  
  
                   
      Tato so naliniṃ    gantvā sītaṃ tuñajarasevitaṃ  
 Soṇḍāya udakamāhatvo    mātaraṃ abhisiñcatha  
  
      Koyaṃ anariyo devo akālena    pi vassati  
 Gato me atrajo putto yo mayhaṃ paricārako  
  
      Uṭṭhehi amma kiṃ sesi āgato tyābhamatrajo  
 Muttomhi kāsirājena vedehena yasassinā  
  
      Ciraṃ jivatu so rājā kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaddhano   yo me puttaṃ amocesi sadā 
 vuddhāpacāyikanti     
   Mātuposakujātakaṃ  
  
   Sallakiyā ca kuṭajā   syā   Nalinaṃ   syā 
   Bhisāmāva   syā hisassamā ca   machasaṃ   Māhitvā   syā machasaṃ   Kaṇṇikārā   
 machasaṃ syā   Akālena pavassati   machasaṃ 
   Tāni   machasaṃ   Raṭṭhavaḍḍhano   machasaṃ syā   Assāyitvāna   machasaṃ    
 Buddhāpacāyikaṃ   machasaṃ vuḍḍhā   syā 
                   
                    
      Suṇohi mayhaṃ vacanaṃ janindi 
 Atthena juṇhambhi idhānupatto  
 Na brāhmaṇe addhike tiṭṭhamāne 
 Gantabbamāhu dipadāna    seṭṭha  
  
      Suṇomi tiṭṭhāmi vadehi brahme 
 Yenāsi    atthena idhānupetto  
 Kaṃ vā tva matthaṃ mayi patthayāno 
 Idhāgamā brahema tadiṅgha brūhi  
  
      Dadāhi me gāmavarāni pañca 
 Dāsisataṃ sattagavaṃ satāni  
 Parosabhassañca suvaṇṇanikkhe 
 Bhariyā ca me sādisi dve dadāhi  
  
                   
      Tapo nu te brāhamaṇa hiṃsarūpo 
 Mantā nu te brāhamaṇa cittarūpā  
 Yakkhāca te assavā santi keci 
 Atthaṃ vā me abhijānāsi kattaṃ  
  
      Na me tapo atthi na cāpi mantā 
 Yakkhāpi    me assavā natthi keci 
 Atthampi te nābhijānāmi kattaṃ 
 Pubbeca kho saṅgatimattamāsi  
  
      Paṭhamaṃ imaṃ dasasnaṃ jānato me 
 Na tābhijānāmi ito puratthā  
 Akkhāhi me pucchito etamatthaṃ 
 Kadā kuhiṃ vā ahu saṅgamo no  
  
      Gandhārarājassa purambhi ramme 
 Avasimhase takkasilāya deva  
 Tatthandhakārambhi timissikāyaṃ    
 Aṃsena aṃsaṃ samaghaṭṭayimha  
  
      Te tattha ṭhatvāna ubho janinda 
 Sārāṇiyaṃ vitisārimbha    tattha  
 Sāyeva no saṃgatimattamāsi 
 Tato na pacchā na pure ahosi  
  
   Dvipadinada   machasaṃ syā   Yenāpi   machasaṃ   Yakkhāca   syā 
   Timissakāyaṃ   syā   Vitisārayimbha   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Yadā dadāci manujesu brahme 
 Samāgamo sappurisena hoti  
 Na paṇḍitā saṅgatisanthavāni 
 Pubbe kataṃ vāpi vināsayanti  
  
      Khālā ca kho saṅgatisanthavāni  
 Pubbe kataṃ vāpi vinasayanti  
 Bahumpi khālesu kataṃ vinassati 
 Tathā hi bālā akataññarūpā  
  
                   
      Dhīrā ca kho saṅgatisanthavāni 
 Pubba kataṃ vāpi na nāsayanti  
 Appampi dhiresu kataṃ na nassati 
 Kathā hi dhīrā sukataññarūpā  
  
      Dadāmi te gāmavarāni pañca 
 Dāsisataṃ santagavaṃ satāni  
 Parosahassañca suvaṇṇanikkhe 
 Bhariyā ca te sādisi dve dadāmi  
  
      Evaṃ sataṃ hoti samecca rāja 
 Nakkhattarājāriva tārakānaṃ  
 Āpurati kāsipati yathā ahaṃ 
 Tayā hi me saṅgamo ajja laddhoti  
   Juṇhajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Yasokaro puññakarohamasmi 
 Sadatthuto samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ 
 Maggāraho devamanussapujito 
 Dhammo ahaṃ dehi adhamma maggaṃ 
  
      Adhammayānaṃ aḷhamāruhitvā 
 Asantasanto balavāhamasmi  
 Sa kissa hetumbhi tavajja dajjaṃ 
 Maggaṃ ahaṃ dhamma adinnapubbaṃ  
  
      Dhammo bhave pāturahosi pubbe 
 Pacchā adhammo udapādi loke  
 Jeṭṭho ca soṭṭho ca sanantano ca 
 Uyyāhi jeṭṭhassa kaniṭṭha maggā  
  
                    
                    
      Na yācanāya napi pāṭirūpā 
 Na arahati    tehaṃ dadeyya    maggaṃ 
 Yuddhañca no hotu ubhinnamajja 
 Yuddhasmi yo jessati tassa maggo  
  
      Sabbā disā anuvisaṭohamasmi    
 Mahabbalo amitayaso atullo    
 Guṇehi sabbehi upetarūpo 
 Dhammo adhamma tvaṃ kathaṃ vijessasi  
  
      Lohena ve bhaññati jātarūpaṃ 
 Na jātarūpena hananti lohaṃ  
 Sace adhammo haññati dhammamajja 
 Ayo suvaṇṇaṃ viya dassaneyyaṃ  
      Sace tuvaṃ yuddhabalo adhamma 
 Na tuyha vaddhā    ca garū ca atthi  
 Maggaṃ ca te dammi piyāppiyena 
 Vācā duruttānipi te khamāmi  
  
                    
      Idañca sutvā vacanaṃ adhammo 
 Avaṃsiro patito uddhapādo  
 Yuddhatthiko ce na labhāmi yuddhaṃ 
 Ettāvatā hoti bhato adhammo  
  
      Khantibalo yuddhabalaṃ vijetavā 
 Hantvā adhammaṃ nihanitvā bhummā  
 Pāyāsi vitto abhiruyha sandanaṃ 
 Maggeneva atibalo saccanikkamo  
  
      Mātāpitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca 
 Asammānitā yassa sake agāre  
 Idheva nikkhippa sariradehaṃ 
 Kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti    
 Yathā adhammo patito avaṃsiro  
  
      Mātāpitā samaṇabrāhmaṇā ca  
 Susammānitā yassa sake agāre  
 Idheva nikkhippa sariradehaṃ 
 Kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti 
 Yathāpi dhammo abhiruyha sandananti  
   Dhammajātakaṃ   
  
   Arahattā   syā   Atulyo  machasaṃ syā 
   Dadeyyaṃ   machasaṃ   Vuḍḍhā   machasaṃ 
   Anuvissaṭo   machasaṃ syā   Vijanti te   machasaṃ 
   Dhammadevaputtajātakaṃ   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
                    
      Ekā nisinnā sucisaññaturu 
 Pāsādamāruyha aninaditaṅgi  
 Yācāmi taṃ kintaranettacakkhu 
 Imekarattiṃ ubhayo vasema  
  
      Ukkiṇaṇantaraparikhaṃ daḷhamaṭṭālakoṭṭhakaṃ  
 Rakkhitaṃ baggahatthehi duppavesamidaṃ puraṃ  
  
      Daharassa yudhino    cāpi āgamo ca na vijjati  
 Atha kena nu vaṇeṇa saṅgamaṃ icchase mayā  
  
                    
      Yakkhohamasmi kalyāṇi āgatosmi tavantikaṃ   tvaṃ maṃ nandaya bhadadante 
 puṇṇakaṃsaṃ dadāmi te  
  
      Devañca yakkhaṃ atha vā manussaṃ 
 Na patthaye udayamaticcamaññaṃ  
 Gaccheva tvaṃ yakkha mahānubhāva 
 Mācassu gantvā punarāvajittha  
  
      Yā sā rati uttamā kāmabhoginaṃ  
 Ratīsu sattā    visamaṃ caranti  
 Mā taṃ ratiṃ jiyi tuvaṃ suvimbhite 
 Dadāmi te rūpiyaṃ kaṃsapuraṃ  
  
                    
      Nāriṃ naro nijjhapayaṃ dhanena 
 Ukkaṃsati yattha karoti chandaṃ  
 Vipaccaṇiko tava deva dhammo 
 Paccakkhato thokatarena esi  
  
      Āyuñca vaṇaṇañca manussaloke 
 Nihiyati    manujānaṃ sugatte  
 Teneva vaṇeṇana dhanampi tuyhaṃ 
 Nihiyati jiṇaṇatarāsi ajja  
  
      Evaṃ me pekkhamānassa rājaputti yasassini  
 Hāyate vata te vaṇeṇā ahorattānamaccaye 
  
      Iminā ca tvaṃ vayasā rājaputti sumedhase  
 Brahmacariyaṃ careyyāsi bhiyyo vaṇaṇavati siyā  
  
   Sucino   samu   Tavantike   machasaṃ   Yaṃhetu sattā   simu 
   Nabhiyyati   machasaṃ  
  
                    
                    
      Dvo na jiranti yathā manussā 
 Gattesu tesaṃ valiyo na honti Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva 
 Kathannu devāna sariradeho  
  
      Dvo na jiranti yathā manussā 
 Gattesu tesaṃ valiyo na honti suce suve bhiyyatarova tesaṃ dibbo ca vaṇeṇā vipulā ca 
 bhogā  
  
                    
      Kiṃsudha hitā janatā anekā maggo ca nekāyatanaṃ pavutto  
 Pucchāmi taṃ yakkha mahānubhāva 
 Kattha ṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye  
  
      Vācaṃ manañca paṇidhāya sammā 
 Kāyena pāpāni akubbamāno 
 Bavhannapānaṃ    gharamāvasanto  
 Saddho mudu saṃvibhāgi vadaññu 
 Saṅgāhako sakhilo saṇhavāco 
 Etthaṭhito paralokaṃ na bhāye  
  
                    
      Anusāsasi maṃ yakkha yathā mātā yathā pitā  
 Uḷāravaṇaṇa pucchāmi konu tvamasi subrahā  
  
      Udayohamasmi kalyāṇi saṅgaratthā idhāgato  
 Āmanna kho taṃgacchāmi muttosmi tava saṅgarā  
  
      Sace kho tvaṃ udayosi saṅgaratthā idhāgato  
 Anusāsa maṃ rājaputta yathāssu puna saṅgamo  
  
      Adhipatati vayo khaṇo tatheva 
 hānaṃ natthi dhuvaṃ   cavanti sattā  
 Parijiyati addhuvaṃ sarīraṃ  
 Udaye mā pamādaṃ carassu dhammaṃ 
  
      Kasiṇā paṭhivi dhanassa purā 
 Ekasseva siyā anaññaveyyā  
 Tañcāpi jahāti avitarāgo 
 Udaye mā pamādaṃ    carassu dhammaṃ  
  
                    
      Mātā ca pitā ca bhātaro ca    
 Bhariyā yāpi dhanena hoti kitā  
 Tecāpi jahanti aññamaññaṃ 
 Udaye mā pamādaṃ carassu dhammaṃ  
  
   Bahunnapānaṃ   machasaṃ   Pamāda machasaṃ   syā 
   Atipatti   syā   Mātā pitā ca bhātaro ca bhagini   syā  
  
                    
      Kayo parabhojananti ñatvā    
 Saṃsāre sugati ca duggati ca  
 Ittaravāsoti jāniyā 
 Udaye mā pamādaṃ carassu dhammaṃ  
  
                    
      Sādhu bhāsatayaṃ    yakkho appaṃ maccāna jīvitaṃ  
 Kasirañca parittañca tañca dukkhena saṃyutaṃ 
 Sāhaṃ ekā pabbajissāmi hitvā kāsiṃ surundhananti  
   Udayajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Mitto mittassa pāniyaṃ adinnaṃ paribhuñajisaṃ    
 Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā 
 Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ kasmā pabbajito ahaṃ  
  
      Paradārañca disvāna chando me adapajjatha  
 Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā 
 Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ  
  
      Pitaramme mahārāja corā agaṇhuṃ kānane  
 Tesāhaṃ pucchito jānaṃ aññathā naṃ viyākariṃ  
  
      Tena pacchā vijigucchiṃ taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā 
 Mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ  
  
      Pāṇātipātamakaruṃ somayāge upaṭṭhite tesāhaṃ samanuññāsiṃ tena pacchā 
 vijigucchiṃ 
 Taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ  
  
                    
      Surāmerayamadhukā yejanā paṭhamāsu no 
 Bahunnate anatthāya majjapānamakappayuṃ Tesāhaṃ samanuññāsiṃ tena pacchā 
 vijigucchiṃ 
 Taṃ pāpaṃ pakataṃ mayā mā puna akaraṃ pāpaṃ tasmā pabbajito ahaṃ  
  
      Dhīratthu subahu kāme duggandhe bahukaṇṭake  
 Ye ahaṃ patisevanno na lahaṃ tādisaṃ sukhaṃ  
  
                    
      Mahassādā sukhā kāmā natthi kāmaparaṃ sukhaṃ  
 Ye kāme patisevanti saggaṃ te upapajjare  
  
   Vicitvā   machasaṃ   syā   Bhāsati   syā   machasaṃ   Paribhuñajissiṃ   machasaṃ   
 Uppajjata   sīmu  
  
                     
      Appassādā dukhā kāmā natthi kāmāparaṃ    dukhaṃ  
 Ye kāme patisevanti nirayaṃ te upapajjare  
  
      Asi yathā sunisito nettiṃsova    supāyiko    
 Sattiva urasi khitto    kāmā dukkhatarā tato  
  
      Aṅgārānaṃva jalitaṃ kāsuṃ sādhikaporisaṃ  
 Phālaṃva divasaṃ tattaṃ kāmā dukkhatarā tato  
  
      Visaṃ yatha halāhalaṃ telamukkaṭṭhitaṃ    yathā  
 Tambaloha vilinaṃva kāmā dukkhatarā tatoti  
   Pānīyajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Mittāmaccaparibbuḷhaṃ ahaṃ vande rathesahaṃ    
 Pabbajissaṃ    mahārāja taṃ devo anumaññatu  
  
      Sace te ūnaṃ kāmehi ahaṃ paripurayāmi te  
 Yo taṃ hiṃsati vāremi mā pabbaji    yudha ñajaya  
  
                    
      Na catthi ūnaṃ kāmehi hiṃsitā me na vijjati  
 Dipañca kātu    micchāmi yaṃ jarā nābhikirati  
  
      Putto vā pitaraṃ yāce pitā vā puttamorasaṃ  
 Negamo yācate tāta mā pabbaṃ yudhañajaya  
  
      Mā maṃ tāta     nivāresi pabbajantaṃ rathesabha  
 Māhaṃ kāmehi sammatto jarāya vasamanvagu    
  
      Ahaṃ taṃ tāta yācāmi ahaṃ putta nivāraye  
 Cirantaṃ daṭṭhumicchāmi mā pabbaji sudhañjaya  
  
                    
      Ussāvova tiṇaggamhi suriyassuggamanaṃ pati  
 Evamāyu manussānaṃ mā maṃ amma nivāraye  
  
   Kāmaparaṃ   simu   Nettiyo   machasaṃ syā   Supāyino   machasaṃ syā   Khittā   
 machasaṃ syā 
   Pakkuṭṭhita   machasaṃ syā   Rathesabha   machasaṃ syā   Pabbajissāmharāja   
 machasaṃ syā   Pabbajji   machasaṃ syā 
   Kattu   syā    Pbbaja   simu    Deci   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Taramāno imaṃ yānaṃ āropetu rathesabha  
 Mā me mātā tarantassa antarāyakarā ahu  
  
      Abhidhāvatha bhaddanne suññaṃ hessati rammakaṃ  
 Yudhañajayo anuññāto sabbadattena rājinā  
  
                    
      Yohu seṭṭho sahassassa    yuvā kañcanasannibho  
 Soyaṃ kumāro pabbajito kāsāyavasano balī  
  
      Ubho kumārā pabbajitā yudhañajayo yudhiṭṭhilo  
 Pahāya mātāpitaro saṅkaṃ chetvāna maccunoti  
   Yudhañjaya jātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Etha lakkhaṇa sitā ca ubho otarathodakaṃ  
 Evāyaṃ bharato āha rājā dasaratho mato  
  
      Kena rāmappabhāvena    socitabbaṃ na socasi  
 Pitaraṃ kālakataṃ sutvā na taṃ pasahate dukhaṃ  
  
      Yaṃ na sakkā pāletuṃ    posena lapatā    bahu  
 Sa kissa viññu medhāvi antānamupatāpaye  
  
                    
      Daharā ca hiye vuddhā ye bālā ye ca paṇḍitā  
 Aḍḍhā ceva daḷiddā ca sabbe maccuparāyaṇā  
  
      Phalānamiva pakkānaṃ niccaṃ papatanā bhayaṃ  
 Evaṃ jātāna maccānaṃ niccaṃ maraṇato bhayaṃ  
  
      Sāyameke na dissanti pāto diṭṭhā bahujjanā  
 Pato eke na dissanti sāyaṃ diṭṭhā bahujjanā 
  
      Paridevayamāno ce kakañci    datthaṃ udabbahe  
 Sammuḷho hiṃsamattānaṃ kayirā cetaṃ vicakkhaṇo  
  
      Kiso vivaṇeṇā bhavati hiṃsamattānamattanā  
 Na tena petā pālenti niratthā paridevanā  
  
   Sahassānaṃ   machasaṃ   Rāma sabhāvena   machasaṃ   Nipāletuṃ   machasaṃ 
   Posenālapataṃ   syā   Kiñci   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Yathāsaraṇamādinnaṃ cārinā parinibbaye  
 Evampi dhīro sutavā medhāvi paṇḍito naro 
 Khippamuppatitaṃ sokaṃ vāto tulaṃva dhaṃsaye  
  
      Ekova macco acceti ekova jāyate kule  
 Saññogaparamātveva sambhogā sabbapāṇinaṃ  
  
      Tasmā hi dhirassa bahussutassa 
 Sampassasato lokamimaṃ parañca  
 Aññāya dhammaṃ bhadayaṃ manañca 
 Sokā mahantāpi na tāpayanti  
  
      Sohaṃ dassañca bhokkhañca    bharissāmi ca ñātake  
 Sesaṃ sampālayissāmi kiccametaṃ vijānato  
  
                    
      Dasa vassasahassāni saṭṭhivassasatāni ca  
 Kambugīvo mahābāhu rāmo rajjamakārayīti 
   Dasarathajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Jānanto no mahārāja tava sīlaṃ janādhipo  
 Ime kumāre pujento na taṃ kenaci maññatha  
  
      Tiṭṭhanne no mahārāje    ādu deve divaṃgate  
 Ñāti naṃ samanumaññiṃsu sampassaṃ atthamantano  
  
      Kena saṃvaravattena sañjate aditiṭṭhasi    
 Kena taṃ nātivattanti ñātisaṅghā samāgatā  
  
      Na rājapunna usuyyāmi samaṇānaṃ mahesinaṃ  
 Sakkaccaṃ te namassāmi pāde vandāmi tādinaṃ  
  
      Te maṃ dhammaguṇe yuttaṃ sussusamanusuyyakaṃ  
 Samaṇā samanusāsanti    Isi dhammaguṇe ratā  
  
      Tesāhaṃ vacanaṃ sutvā samaṇānaṃ mahesinaṃ  
 Na kiñci atimaññāmi dhamme me nirato mano  
  
      Hatthāruhā    aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārikā  
 Tesaṃ nappaṭibandhāmi nibaddhaṃ bhattavetanaṃ    
  
   Sohaṃ yasañca bhogañca   machasaṃ syā   Mahārāja   machasaṃ 
   Abhinatiṭṭhasi   machasaṃ syā   Manusāsanti   machasaṃ 
   Hatthārohā   machasaṃ syā   Tiviṭṭhaṃ bhatta vetanaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
  
      Mahāmattā ca me atthi mantino paricārakā    
 Bārāṇasiṃ voharanti bahumaṃsa    surodakaṃ  
  
                    
      Athopi vāṇijā phitā nānā raṭṭhehi āgatā  
 Tesu me vihitā rakkhā evaṃ jānāhuposatha  
  
      Dhammena kira ñātinaṃ rajjaṃ kārehi saṃvara  
 Medhāvi paṇḍito cāpi    athopi ñātinaṃ hito 
  
      Taṃ taṃ ñāti paribbuḷhaṃ nānāratanamocitaṃ  
 Amittā nappasahanti indaṃva asurādhipoti  
   Saṃvarajākataṃ  
  
                    
      Ummujjanti nimujjanti manussā khuranāsikā  
 Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma samuddo katamo ayaṃ  
  
      Bharukacchā payātānaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ  
 Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya khuramāliti vuccata  
      Yathā aggiva suriyo va  samuddo pati  dissati   
 Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma samuddo katamo ayaṃ  
  
                    
      Bharukacchā payātānaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ  
 Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya aggimāliti vuccati  
  
      Yathā dadhiṃva khiraṃva samuddo pati    dissati  
 Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma samuddo katamo ayaṃ  
  
      Bharukacchā payātānaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ  
 Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya dadhimāliti vuccati  
  
      Yathākusova sassova    samuddo pati dissati  
 Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma samuddo katamo ayaṃ  
  
      Bharukacchā payātānaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ  
 Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya dadhimāliti vuccati  
  
   Paricārikā   machasaṃ syā   Bahuṃmaṃsaṃ   syā   Cāsi   machasaṃ syā 
   Yathā aggiva suriyo   machasaṃ yathā aggisuriyo   syā   Paṭi   machasaṃ syā 
   Ca   syā  
  
                     
                    
      Yathā naḷova veluva samuddo pati dissati  
 Suppārakaṃ taṃ pucchāma samuddo katamo ayaṃ  
      Bharukacchā payātānaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ  
 Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya naḷimāliti vuccati  
  
      Bharukacchā payātānaṃ vāṇijānaṃ dhanesinaṃ 
 Nāvāya vippanaṭṭhāya vaḷavāmukhiti vuccati  
  
                    
      Yato sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattosmi viññutaṃ  
 Nābhijānāmi sañcicca ekapāṇampi hiṃsitaṃ  
 Etena saccavajjena sotthiṃ nāvā nivattatuti  
   Suppārakajātakaṃ  
  
 Ekādasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Siri mātusuposaka nāgavaro 
 Puna juṇha adhamma mudayavaro  
 Atha pāṇiyudhañajayako ca dasa 
 Ratha saṃvara pāragatena navāti  
  
   Mabhabbhayo   machasaṃ   Saddo   machasaṃ   Suyyati   machasaṃ  
  
                    
                    
      Khuddānaṃ lahucittānaṃ akataññuna dubhinaṃ    
 Nādevasatto puriso ṭhinaṃ saddhātumarahati  
  
      Na tā pajānanti kataṃ na kiccaṃ 
 Na mātaraṃ pitaraṃ bhātaraṃ vā  
 Anariyā samatikkannadhammā 
 Sasseva cittassa vasaṃ vajanti  
  
      Cirānuvuttampi    piyaṃ manāpaṃ 
 Anukampaṃ pāṇasamampi    santaṃ  
 Āvāsu kiccesu ca naṃ jahanti 
 Tasmāhamitthinaṃ na vissasāmi  
  
      Thinañhi cittaṃ yathā vānarassa 
 Kantappakantaṃ    yathā rukkhachāyā  
 Calācalaṃ bhadayaṃ itthiyānaṃ 
 Cakkassa nemi viya parivantati  
  
      Yadā tā passanti samekkhamānā 
 Ādeyyarūpaṃ purisassa vittaṃ saṇhāhi vācāhi nayanti menaṃ 
 Kambojakā jalajeneva assaṃ  
  
      Yadā tā passanti samekkhamānā 
 Ādeyyarūpaṃ purisassa vittaṃ saṇamannāgato naṃ parivajjayanti  
 Tiṇṇo nadipāragatova kullaṃ  
  
      Silesupamā    sikhiriva sabbabhakkhā 
 Tikkhamāyā    nadiriva sighasotā    
 Sevanti hetā piyamappiyañca 
 Nāgaṃ yathā orakulaṃ parañca  
  
      Na tā ekassa na davinnaṃ āpaṇova pasārito    
 Yo tā mayhanti maññeyya vātaṃ jalena bādhaye  
  
   Dubbhinaṃ   machasaṃ dunabbhiṃ   syā   Cirānu vuṭṭhambhi   machasaṃ cirānu 
 vuṭṭhampi  vi   Pāṇasamampi bhattuṃ   vi Machasaṃ   kaṇṇappakaṇṇaṃ   vi   
 Lesupamā   machasaṃ   Tikkhasinā   vi machasaṃ   Siṅghasotā   machasaṃ   Āpaṇo so   
 machasaṃ vi  
  
                    
      Yathā nidi ca pantho ca pānāgāraṃ sabhā papā  
 Evaṃ lokitthiyo nāma velā tāsaṃ na vijjati  
  
      Ghatāsanasamāhetā kaṇhasappa sirūpamā  
 Gave bahi tiṇasseva omasanti varaṃ varaṃ  
  
      Ghatāsanaṃ kuñajariṃ kaṇhasappaṃ 
 Muddhāhisittaṃ pamadā ca sabbā  
 Ete naro niccayatto    bhajetha 
 Tesaṃ bhave dubbidu sabbabhāvo    
  
      Nāccantavaṇaṇā na bahunaṃ    kantā 
 Na dakkhiṇā pamadā sevitabbā  
 Na parassa bhariyā na dhanassa hetu 
 Etitthiyo pañca na sevitabbāti  
   Cuḷakuṇālajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Kā tvaṃ suddhehi vatthehi aghe vehāsayaṃ ṭhitā  
 Kena tyāssuni vattanti kuto taṃ bhayamāgataṃ  
  
      Taveva deva vijite bhaddasāloti maṃ vidu  
 Saṭṭhiṃ vassasahassāni tiṭṭhato pujitassa me  
  
      Kārayantā nagarāni agāre ca disampati  
 Vivadhe cāpi pāsāde na manne avavamaññisuṃ  
 Yatheva maṃ te pujesuṃ tatheva tvampi pujaya  
  
                    
      Tava ahaṃ na passāmi thullaṃ kāyena te dumaṃ  
 Ārohapariṇāhena abhirūposi jātiyā  
  
      Pāsādaṃ kārayissāmi ekatthambhaṃ manoramaṃ  
 Tattha taṃ upanessāmi ciraṃ te yakkha jīvitaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ cittaṃ    udapādi sarirena vinābhāvo  
 Puthuso maṃ vikantetvā khaṇḍaso avakantatha 
  
   Niccayato   machasaṃ syā   Sabbabhāvoya   machasaṃ   Naccattavaṇaṇanaṃ bahunaṃ 
   maramma   Evaṃ hetaṃ   vi  
  
                    
                     
      Agge ca chetvā majjhe ca pacchā    mulaññaca jindatha  
 Evaṃ me chijjamānassa na dukkhaṃ maraṇaṃ siyā  
  
      Hatthapādaṃ    yathā chinde kaṇaṇanāsañca jivite    
 Tato pacchā siro chinde taṃ dukkhaṃ maraṇaṃ siyā  
  
      Sukhannu khaṇḍaso chinnaṃ    bhaddasāla vanaspati    
 Ki hetu kiṃ    upādāya khaṇḍaso chinnamicchasi  
  
      Yañca hetuṃ upādāya hetu    dhammupasaṃhitaṃ 
 Khaṇḍaso chinnamicchāmi mahārāja suṇohi me  
      Ñāti    me sukhasaṃvaddhā mama passe nivātajā 
 Te pihaṃ upahiṃseyyaṃ paresaṃ asukhovitaṃ    
  
                    
      Cetabbarūpaṃ     cetesi     bhaddasāla vanasapati  
 Hitakāmosi ñātinaṃ abhayaṃ samma dadāmi teti  
   Bhaddasāla jātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Kasanti vapanti     te janā 
 Manujā kammaphalupajivino  
 Nayimassa dipakassa bhāgino 
 Jambudipā idameva no varaṃ  
  
                    
      Tipañcarattupagamambhi cande 
 Vogo hā hohiti sāgarassa     
 Upalāpayaṃ dipamimaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 Mā vo vadhi gacchatha leṇamaññaṃ  
  
      Na jātayaṃ     sāgaravārivego 
 Uppāṭaye     dipamimaṃ uḷāraṃ  
 Taṃ me nimittehi bahuhi diṭṭhaṃ 
 Mā bhetha kiṃ socatha modathambho     
  
   Pacchā mulaṃ vi vicindatha mulambhi chindatha   machasaṃ syā 
   Hatthapāde   machasaṃ    Ceteyya rūpaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Jivato   machasaṃ jivito   vi    Cetayi   nā  
   Chanda   syā    Vappana   machasaṃ 
   Vanappati   machasaṃ syā    Rasassa   vi 
   Taṃ   vi    Na jātuyaṃ   machasaṃ syā  
   Hetu   vi machasaṃ syā    Upalaṃ vassaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Ñāti   vi machasaṃ syā    Modatha vo   machasaṃ 
   Assaṃ dukhovitaṃ   vi  
  
                    
      Pahutabhakkhaṃ    bahuannapānaṃ 
 Pattattha    āvāsamimaṃ uḷāraṃ  
 Na vo bhayaṃ paṭipassāmi kiñci 
 Āputta puttehi pamodathavho    
  
                    
      Yo tvevayaṃ dakkhiṇassaṃ disāyaṃ 
 Khemanti pakkosati tassa saccaṃ  
 Na uttaro vedi bhayāhayassa 
 Mā bhetha kiṃ sovatha modathambho  
  
      Yathā ime vippavadanti yakkhā 
 Eko bhayaṃ saṃsati khemameko 
 Tadiṅgha mayhaṃ vacanaṃ suṇātha  
 Khippaṃ lahuṃ mā vinassimbha    sabbe 
  
      Sabbe samāgamma karoma nāvaṃ 
 Doṇiṃ daḷhaṃ sabbayantupapannaṃ  
 Sace ayaṃ dakkhiṇo saccamāha 
 Moghaṃ paṭikkosati utataro ayaṃ  
  
      Sace vano hohiti    āpadatthā 
 Imañca dipaṃ na pariccajema  
 Sace ca kho uttaro saccamāha 
 Moghaṃ paṭikkosati dakkhiṇo ayaṃ    
 Tameva nāvaṃ abhiruyha sabbe 
 Evaṃ mayaṃ sotthi tāremu pāraṃ  
  
                    
      Na ce sugaṇhaṃ paṭhamena seṭṭhaṃ 
 Kaniṭṭha māpāthagataṃ gahetvā 
 Yo cidha majjhaṃ    paṭiceyya gaṇhati  
 Sace nāro seṭṭhamupeti ṭhānaṃ 
  
                    
      Yathāpi te sāgaravārimajjhe 
 Sakammunā    sotthiṃ vahiṃsu vāṇijā  
 Anāgatatthaṃ paṭivijjhiyāna 
 Appampi nāccetisa bhuripañño    
  
   Bahutta   machasaṃ   Pattatha patattha   machasaṃ   Pamodatha vo   machasaṃ 
   Vinasimbha   vi machasaṃ syā   Hehiti   machasaṃ syā 
   Dakkhiṇu   machasaṃ   Tacchaṃ   machasaṃ   Sakammanā   sīmu   So   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Bālā ca mohena rasānugiddhā 
 Anāgataṃ appaṭivijjhiyatthaṃ  
 Paccuppanne sidanti atthajate    
 Samuddamajjhe yathā te manussā  
  
                    
      Anāgataṃ paṭikayirātha kiccaṃ 
 Māmaṃ kiccaṃ kiccakāle vyadhesi  
 Taṃ tādisaṃ paṭigata    kiccakāriṃ 
 Na taṃ kiccaṃ kiccakāle vyadheti  
   Samuddavāṇija jātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Kāmaṃ kāmayamānassa tassa ve taṃ samijjhati  
 Addhā pitimano hoti laddhā macco yadicchati  
  
      Kāmaṃ kāmayamānassa tassa ve taṃ samijjhati  
 Tato naṃ aparaṃ kāme ghamme taṇhaṃva vindati  
  
      Gavaṃva siṅgino saṅgaṃ vaḍḍhamānassa vaḍḍhati  
 Evaṃ mandassa posassa bālassa avijānato  
 Bhiyyo taṇhā pipāsā ca vaḍḍhamānassa vaḍḍhati  
  
      Pathavyā sāliyavakaṃ gavāssaṃ    dāsaporisaṃ  
 Datvāpi    nālamekassa iti vidvā samañcare  
      Rājā pasayha paṭhavaṃ    vijetvā    
 Sasāgarantaṃ mahimāvasanno  
 Oraṃ samuddassa atittarūpo 
 Pāraṃ samuddassapi patthayetha  
  
      Yāva anussaraṃ    kāme manasā titti nājjhagā  
 Tato nivattā    paṭikkamma    disvā  
 Te ve tittā ye paññāya tittā  
  
   Atthe   vi   Paṭikataṃ   machasaṃ paṭikata   syā 
   Gavassa   machasaṃ   Datvā vā   viṃ  
   Pathaviṃ   machasaṃ   Vijitvā   machasaṃ 
   Yo va anussaraṃ   vi yo ca manussaraṃ   machasaṃ   Nivatvā   vi   Paṭikammaṃ  
  
                    
      Paññāya tittinaṃ seṭṭhaṃ na so kāmehi tappati  
 Paññāya tittaṃ    purisaṃ taṇhā na kurute vasaṃ  
  
      Apacineteva kāmāni    appicchassa    alolupo  
 Samuddamatto puriso na so kāmehi tappati  
  
                    
      Rathakārova cammassa parikattaṃ apāhanaṃ  
 Yaṃ yaṃ cajati    kāmānaṃ taṃ taṃ sampajjate sukhaṃ  
 Sabbeñca sukhamiccheyya sabbe kāme pariccaje  
  
      Aṭṭha te bhāsitā gāthā sabbā honti sahassiyo  
 Patigaṇha mahābrahme sādhetaṃ tava bhāsitaṃ  
  
      Na me attho sahassehi satehi nahutehi vā  
 Pacchimaṃ bhāsato gāthaṃ kāme me na rato mano  
  
      Bhaddo    vatāyaṃ māṇavako sabbalokavidu muni  
 Yo taṇhaṃ    dukkhajananiṃ parijānāti paṇḍitoti  
   Kāmajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Dasa balu imāni    ṭhānāni yāni pubbe akāritvā  
 Sa pacchā manutappati iccāha rājā janasandho  
  
      Aladdhā cittaṃ tapati    pubbe asamudānitaṃ 
 Ka pubbe dhanamesissaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Sakyarūpaṃ pure santaṃ mayā sippaṃ na sikkhitaṃ  
 Kicchā vutti asippassa iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Kuṭavedi pure āsiṃ pisuno piṭṭhimaṃsiko  
 Caṇḍo ca pharuso cāsiṃ    iti pacchānutappati  
  
                    
      Pāṇātipāti pure āsiṃ luddo cāsiṃ   anāriyo  
 Bhūtānaṃ nāvadāyissaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Bahūsu vata santisu anapādāsu itthisu  
 Paradāraṃ asevissaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
   Sutittā   machasaṃ   Kāmānaṃ   machasaṃ   Apicchasya   machasaṃ   Jahati   
 machasaṃ syā   Bhaddako   machasaṃ syā   Yo imaṃ taṇṭhiṃ vi   Dasabalumāni   syā   
 Aladdāvicittaṃ tappati   machasaṃ   Ca pi   machasaṃ    Cāsi   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Bahumbhi vata santambhi annapāte upaṭṭhite  
 Na pubbe adadiṃ dānaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vāpi jiṇaṇake gatayobbane    
 Pahu santo na posissaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Ācariyamanusatthāraṃ sabbakāmarasāharaṃ  
 Pitaraṃ atimaññissaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi silavante bahussute  
 Na pubbe payirupāsissaṃ iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Sādhu hoti tapo ciṇeṇā santo ca payirupāsito  
 Na ca pubbe tapo ciṇeṇā iti pacchānutappati  
  
      Yo ca etāni ṭhanāni yoniso paṭipajjati  
 Karaṃ purisakiccāni sa pacchā nānutappatīti  
   Janasandha jākataṃ  
  
                    
      Kaṇho kaṇo ca ghoro ca sukkadāṭho patāpavā    
 Baddho pañcahi rajajuhi kiṃ dhira sunakho tava  
  
      Kāyaṃ migānaṃ atthāya asinara    bhavissati  
 Manussānaṃ anayo hutvā tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
                    
      Pattahatthā samaṇakā muṇḍā saṃghāṭi pārutā  
 Naṅgalehi kasissanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Tapassiniyo pabbajitā muṇḍā saṃghāṭi pārutā  
 Yadā loke gamissanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Dīghuttaroṭā    jaṭilā paṅkadantā rajasirā  
 Iṇaṃ vodāya gacchanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Adhicca vede    sāvittiṃ yaññatanatrañca    brahmaṇā  
 Bhatikāya yajissanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
  
   Jinanakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ   machasaṃ   Pabhāsavā   machasaṃ syā 
   Usinnara   syā   Dīghottaroṭṭha   machasaṃ 
   Vedaṃ   machasaṃ   Yaññātannañca   machasaṃ yaññaṃ tantuñca  syā 
  
                    
      Mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vāpi jiṇaṇake gatayobbane    
 Pahu santā na bharanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vāpi jiṇaṇake gatayobbane  
 Bālā tumbheti vakkhanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Ācariyabhariyaṃ sakhābhariyaṃ    mātulāniṃ pitucchayaṃ   yadā loke gamissanti tadā 
 kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Asicammaṃ gahetvāna khaggaṃ paggayha brāhmaṇā 
 Patthaghātaṃ    karissanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Sukkacchavi vedhaverā thullabāhu apātubhā  
 Mithubhedaṃ karissanti tadā kaṇho pamokkhati  
  
      Māyāvino nekatikā asappurisacintakā  
 Yadā loke bhavissanti tadā kaṇho pamekkhatiti  
   Mahākaṇha jātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Neva kiṇāmi napi vikkiṇāmi 
 Na cāpi me sannicayo ca atthi  
 Sukiccharūpaṃ vatidaṃ parittaṃ  
 Patthodano nālamayaṃ duvinnaṃ  
  
      Appambhā appakaṃ dajjaṃ anumajjhato majjhakaṃ  
 Bahumbhā bahukaṃ dajjā adānaṃ nupapajjati  
  
      Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja ca  
 Ariyaṃ maggaṃ samāruha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ 
  
   Jinanakaṃ gatayobbanaṃ   machasaṃ   Sakhiṃ   machasaṃ   Pitucchakiṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Panthaghāṭaṃ   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Moghañcassa hutaṃ hoti moghañcāpi samihitaṃ  
 Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ  
  
      Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja ca  
 Arayaṃ maggaṃ samāruha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  
  
      Saccaṃ tassa    hutaṃ hoti saccaṃ cāpi samihitaṃ  
 Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ  
      Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja ca  
 Ariyaṃ maggaṃ samāruha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  
  
      Sarañca juhati poso khāhukāya gayāya ca  
 Doṇe timbarutitthasmiṃ sighasote    mahāvahe  
  
      Atra cassa hoti atra cassa samihitaṃ  
 Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ neko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ  
      Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja ca  
 Ariyaṃ maggaṃ samāruha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  
      Khiḷisaṃ hi so niggilati    dighasuttaṃ sabandhanaṃ  
 Atithismiṃ yo nisinnasmiṃ eko bhuñjati bhojanaṃ  
      Taṃ taṃ vadāmi kosiya dehi dānāni bhuñja ca  
 Ariyaṃ maggaṃ samāruha nekāsi labhate sukhaṃ  
  
      Uḷāravaṇaṇā vata brāhmaṇā ime  
 Ayañca vo suta kho kissa hetu  
 Uccāvacaṃ vaṇaṇanihaṃ vikubbati 
 Akkhātha no brāhmaṇā ke nu tumbhe  
  
   Saccañcassa   vi   Nekopi   machasaṃ syā   Siṅgasote   machasaṃ 
   Nigilati   machasaṃ syā 
  
  
                     
      Cando ca suriyo ca ubho idhāgatā 
 Ayaṃ pana mātali deva sārathi  
 Sakkohamasmi tidasānamindo 
 Eso ca kho pañcasikhoti vuccati  
  
      Pāṇissarā mudiṅgā ca murajāḷambarāni ca  
 Suttamenaṃ pabodhenti paṭibuddho ca nandati  
  
      Ye kecime maccharino kadariyā 
 Paribhāsakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ  
 Idheva nikkhippa sariradehaṃ 
 Kāyassa bhedā nirayaṃ vajanti  
  
      Ye kecime suggatimāsasānaṃ     
 Dhamme ṭhitā saṃyame saṃvibhāge  
 Idheva nikkhippa sariradehaṃ 
 Kāyassa bhedā sugatiṃ vajanti  
  
      Tvaṃ nosi ñāti purimāsu jātisu 
 So macchari rosako pāpadhammo  
 Taveva atthāya idhāgatambhā Mā pāpadhammo nirayaṃ apattha  
  
      Esāhamajjeva apāramāmi 
 Nacāpahaṃ kiñci kareyya pāpaṃ  
 Nacāpi me kiñcimadeyyamatthi 
 Navāpadatvā udakampahaṃ pibe    
  
      Evañca me dadato sabbakālaṃ 
 Bhogā ime vāsava khiyissanti  
 Tato ahaṃ pabbajissāmi pakka 
 Hitvāna kāmāni yathodhikāniti  
   Kosiyajātakaṃ  
  
   Māsamātā   vi machasaṃ   Tavāpi datvā udakaṃ picāmi   machasaṃ vi  
  
                    
      Yesaṃ na kadāci bhūtapubbaṃ    
 Sakkhiṃ sattapadampi imasmiṃ loke  
 Jātā amittā    duve sabhāyā 
 Paṭisandhāya caranti kissa hetu  
  
      Yadi me ajja pātarāsakāle 
 Paṇhaṃ na sakkuṇeyyātha vattumetaṃ  
 Raṭṭhā pabbājayissāmi vo sabbe 
 Nahi mattho dupapaññajātikehi  
  
      Mahājanasamāgamambhi ghore 
 Janagolāhalasaṅgamambhi jate 
 Vikkhittamanā anekavacittā 
 Pañhaṃ na sakkuṇoma vattumetaṃ  
  
      Ekaggacittā ca ekamekā 
 Rahasigatā atthuṃ nicinnayitvā  
 Paviveke sammasitvāna dhīrā 
 Atha vakkhanti janinda atthametaṃ  
  
      Uggaputtarājaputtiyānaṃ 
 Urabbhamaṃsaṃ piyaṃ manāpaṃ  
 Na te sunakhassa adenti maṃsaṃ 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  
  
      Cammaṃ vibhananti phaḷakassa 
 Assapiṭṭhattharaṇasukhassa hetu  
 Naca te sunakhassa attharanti 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  
  
      Āvellikasiṅgiko hi meṇḍo 
 Na ca sunakhassa visāṇāni    atthi  
 Tiṇahakkho maṃsabhojano ca 
 Atha meṇḍassa suṇena sabyamassa  
  
      Tiṇamāsi palāsamāsi meṇḍo 
 Na ca sunakho tiṇamāsi no palāsaṃ  
 Gaṇheyya suṇo sasaṃ khiḷāraṃ 
 Atha meṇaḍassa suṇena saṇyamassa  
  
   Sutapubbaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Jātāmittā   machasaṃ   Visānakāni   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Aḍḍhaṭṭhapādo catuppadassa 
 Meṇḍo aṭṭhanakho adissamāno  
 Chādiyamāharati ayaṃ imassa 
 Maṃsaṃ āharati ayaṃ amussa  
  
      Pāsādagato videhaseṭṭho 
 Vitihāraṃ aññamaññabhojanānaṃ  
 Addakkhi kira sakkhi taṃ janindo 
 Khobhukkhassa ca puṇaṇamukhassa cetaṃ  
  
      Lābhā vata me anapparūpā 
 Yassa medisā paṇḍatā kulambhi  
 Pañcassa gambhiragataṃ nipuṇamatthaṃ 
 Paṭivijjhanti subhāsitena dhīrā  
  
      Assatarirathañca ekamekaṃ 
 Phītaṃ gāmavarañca ekamekaṃ  
 Sabbesaṃ vo dammi paṇḍitānaṃ  
 Paramapatitamano subhāsitenāti  
   Meṇḍakapañho  
  
                    
      Nādiṭṭhā    parato dosaṃ aṇuṃthulāni sabbaso  
 Issaro paṇaye daṇḍaṃ sāmaṃ appaṭivekkhiya  
  
      Yo ca appaṭivekkhitvā daṇḍaṃ kubbati khattiyo  
 Sakaṇṭakaṃ so gilati jaccandhova samakkhikaṃ  
  
      Adaṇḍiyaṃ daṇḍiyati daṇḍiyañca adaṇḍiyaṃ 
 Andhova visamaṃ maggaṃ na jānāti samāsamaṃ  
  
      Yo ca etāni ṭhānāni aṇuṃthulāni sabbaso  
 Sudiṭṭhaṃ cānusāseyya sace voharitumarahati    
  
      Nekantamudunā sakkā ekantatikhiṇena vā  
 Attaṃ mahanne ṭhāpetuṃ    tasmā ubhayamācare  
  
   Nā daṭṭhā   vi   Sace mohātu   vi   hāpetuṃ   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Paribhuto mudu hoti atitikkho ca veravā  
 Etañca ubhayaṃ ñatvā anumajjhaṃ samācare  
  
      Bahumpi ratto bhāseyya duṭṭhopi bahubhāsati  
 Na itthikāraṇā rāja puttaṃ ghātetumarahasi  
  
                    
      Sabbo ca loko ekanto    itthi ca ayamekikā  
 Tenāhaṃ paṭipajjassaṃ gaccha pakkhipatheva naṃ  
  
                    
      Anekatāle narake gamibhire ca suduttare  
 Pātito giriduggasmiṃ kena tvaṃ tattha nāmari  
  
      Nāgo nāgabalo    tattha thāmavā girisānujo  
 Paccaggahi maṃ bhogehi tenāhaṃ tattha nāmari  
  
      Ehi taṃ paṭinessāmi rājaputta sakaṃ gharaṃ  
 Ejjaṃ kāresi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
      Yathā gilitvā baḷisaṃ uddhareyya salohitaṃ  
 Uddharitvā sukhī assa    evaṃ passāmi attanaṃ  
  
      Kinnu tvaṃ baḷisaṃ brūsi kiṃ tvaṃ brūsi salohitaṃ  
 Kinnu tvaṃ ubbhataṃ brūsi tamme akkhāhi pucchito  
      Kāmāhaṃ baḷisaṃ brūmi hatthiassaṃ salohitaṃ  
 Cattāhaṃ abbhataṃ brūmi evaṃ jānāhi khattiya  
  
                    
      Ciñcāmāṇavikā mātā devadatto ca me pitā  
 Akando paṇḍito nāgo sāriputto ca devatā  
 Ahaṃ tadā rājaputto    evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti  
   Mahāpadumajātakaṃ  
  
   Ekato   machasaṃ syā   Nāgo jātapaṇo tattha nā phaṇo   machasaṃ   Sukhaṃ passāmi 
 attani   machasaṃ   Rājaputto ahaṃ āsiṃ   vi machasaṃ  
  
                    
                    
      Kāni kammāni kubbānaṃ kathaṃ viññu parakkame 
 Amittaṃ jāneyya medhāvi disvā sutvā paṇḍito 
  
      Na taṃ umbhayate disvā na ca naṃ paṭinandati  
 Cakkhuni cassa    na dadāti paṭilomaṃ ca vattati  
  
      Amitte tassa bhajati mitte tassa na sevati  
 Vaṇaṇakāme nivāreti akkosante pasaṃsati  
  
      Guyhañca tassa nakkhāti tassa guyhaṃ na guhati  
 Kammaṃ tasasa na vaṇeṇatipaññassa nappasaṃsati  
  
      Ahave nandati tassa bhave tassa na nandati  
 Acchariyaṃ bhojanaṃ laddhā tassa nuppajjate sati  
 Tato taṃ nānukampati aho sopi labheyayito    
  
      Iccete soḷasākārā amittasmiṃ patiṭṭhitā  
 Yehi amittaṃ jāneyya disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito  
  
                    
      Kāni kammāni kubbānaṃ kathaṃ viññu parakkame  
 Mittaṃ jāneyya medhāvi disvā sutvā ca paṇḍito  
  
      Pavuttaṃ    cassa sarati āgataṃ abhinandati  
 Tato kelāyito hoti vācāya paṭinandati  
  
      Mitte tasseva bhajati amitte tassa na sevati  
 Akosante nivārati vaṇaṇakāme pasaṃsati  
  
      Guhyañca tassa akkhāti tassa guyhañca guhati  
 Kammañca tassa vaṇeṇati paññaṃ tassa    pasaṃsati  
  
   Cakkhuni tassa vi tissa   machasaṃ   Labheyyato   vi 
   Pavuṭṭhaṃ tassa   machasaṃ pavutthaṃ taṃ   vi   Paññamasasa   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Bhave ca nandati tassa abhatva tassa na nandati  
 Acchariyaṃ bhojanaṃ laddhā tassa uppajjate sati  
 Tato taṃ anukampati aho sopi    labheyayito  
      Iccete soḷasākārā mittasmiṃ suppatiṭṭhitā  
 Yehi mittaṃ ca jāneyya disvā sutvā ca paṇḍitoti  
    Mittāmittajātakaṃ  
  
 Dvādasakanipāto niṭṭhito 
  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Lahucitta sāsāla kasanti puna 
 Atha kāma dasabaluṭṭhāna varo  
 Atha kaṇha sukosiya meṇḍavaro 
 Padumo puna mittavāre dasa  
  
   Pahāsopi   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
                     
 Terasaka nipāto 
                    
      Abhāsi me ambapalāni pubbe 
 Aṇuni thulāni ca brahmacāri  
 Teheva mantehi nadāni tuyhaṃ 
 Dumapphalā pātubhavanti brahme  
  
      Nakkhattayogaṃ paṭimānayāmi    
 Khaṇaṃ muhuttaṃ na maṃ tosayanti    
 Nakkhantayogañca khaṇañca laddhā 
 Athā    harissambaphalaṃ pahutaṃ    
  
                    
      Nakkhattayogaṃ na pure abhāṇi 
 Khaṇaṃ muhuttaṃ na pure asaṃsi  
 Athāhari    ambaphalaṃ pahutaṃ 
 Vaṇeṇana gandhena rasenupetaṃ  
  
      Mantāhijappena parassa    tuyhaṃ 
 Dumapphalā pātubhavanti brahme  
 Svājjana pāresi japampi mante    
 Ayaṃ so ko nāma tavajja dhammo  
  
      Caṇḍālaputto mama sampadāsa 
 Dhammena manne pakatiñca saṃsi  
 Mā cassu me pucchito nāmagontaṃ  
 Guyhittho mā taṃ vijaheyya    manno  
  
      Sohaṃ janindena janamhi puṭṭho 
 Makkhāhibhuto alikaṃ abhāsiṃ  
 Mantā ime brāhmaṇassāti micchā 
 Pahinamanto kapaṇo rudāmi  
  
                    
      Pharaṇḍā pucimandā vā athavā pāḷibhaddakā  
 Madhuṃ madhutthiko vinde so tassa dumuttamo  
  
   Patimānayāmi   mi machasaṃ   Maṇaṃmuhuttaṃ mannena passaṃmachasaṃ   Addhā   
 machasaṃ syā   Bahunaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Sayaṃ hari   machasaṃ   Purehi   machasaṃ 
 syā   Svajja na pādesi jappampi mantaṃ   machasaṃ   Vijaheyyu   syā 
  
                    
      Khattiyā brāhmaṇā vessā suddā caṇḍālapukkusā  
 Yasmā    dhammā vijāneyya so hi tassa naruttamo  
  
      Imassa daṇḍañca vadhañca datvā 
 Gale gahetvā balayātha jammaṃ  
 Yo uttamatthaṃ kasirena laddhaṃ 
 Mānātimānena vināsayittha  
                    
      Yathā samaṃ maññamāno pateyya 
 Sobbhaṃ guhaṃ narakaṃ putipādaṃ  
 Rajjuni vā akkame kaṇhasappaṃ 
 Andho yathā jotimadhiṭṭhaheyya    
 Evampi maṃ tvaṃ khalitaṃ sapañña    
 Pahinamantassa punappasida    
  
      Dhammena maneta    tava sampadāsiṃ 
 Tuvampi dhammena paṭiggahesi 
 Pakatimpi te attamano asaṃsiṃ    
 Dhamme ṭhitaṃ taṃ na jaheyya manto  
  
                    
      So bāla mantaṃ kasirena laddhaṃ 
 Yaṃ dulalhaṃ ajja manussaloke  
 Kicchā laddhā jivikaṃ appapañño    
 Vināsayi alikaṃ bhāsamāno  
  
      Bālassa muḷhassa aññukatano ca 
 Musā bhaṇantassa asasaññatassa  
 Mante mayaṃ tādisake na dema 
 Kuto mantā gaccha na mayha ruccasiti  
   Ambajātakaṃ  
  
   Yamhā   machasaṃ syā   Andho yathā jotiṃ paviṭṭhaheyya   machasaṃ   Sapaññaṃ   vi 
   Punappadāhi   machasaṃ sampadāhi   syā   Mattaṃ   machasaṃ   Asaṃsi   mi machasaṃ 
 syā   Kiñcāpi laddhā jīvituṃ appapañño   machasaṃ vi kicchāpi laddhā jīvitaṃ appa paññā 
   syā  
  
                    
                    
      Kuṭhārihattho puriso vanamogayha tiṭṭhasi    
 Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kiṃ dāruṃ chetumicchasi  
  
                    
      Isso    vanāni carasi samāni visamāni ca  
 Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kiṃ dāruṃ nemiyā daḷhaṃ 
  
      Neva sālo na khadhiro nāssakaṇeṇakuto dhavo    
 Rukkhova endano nāma taṃ dāruṃ nemiyā daḷahanti  
      Kidisānissa pattāni khandho vā pana kidiso  
 Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi yathā jānemu endanaṃ  
  
      Yassa sākhā palambanti namanti na ca bhañajare  
 So rukkho endato nāma yassa mule ahaṃ    ṭhito  
  
      Arānaṃ cakkanāhinaṃ īsānemi rathassa ca  
 Sabbassa te kammaniyo ayaṃ hessati endano  
  
                    
      Iti endanarukkhopi tāvade ajjhabhāsatha  
 Mayhampi vacanaṃ atthi bhāradvāja suṇohi me  
  
      Issassa    upakhandhambhā    okkacca caturaṅgulaṃ  
 Tena nemiṃ pariharesi    evaṃ daḷhataraṃ siyā 
  
      Iti endanarukkhopi veraṃ appesi    tāvade jātānañca ajānānaṃ issānaṃ dukkhamāvahi 
     
  
                    
      Icceva    endano issaṃ isso    ca pana endanaṃ 
 Aññamaññaṃ vivādena aññamaññamaghātayuṃ  
  
      Evameva manussesu vivādo yattha jāyati  
 Mayuranavacaṃ naccanti yathā te issaphandanā      
  
   Tiṭṭhati   vi   Īso   syā iso   simu 
   Nassa kaṇeṇa kakuyovā   machasaṃ   Savāhaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Imassa   machasaṃ syā   Upakkhanadhamhā   machasaṃ 
   Pahāresi   machasaṃ   Appeti   machasaṃ kappesi   syā 
   Devatā   syā    Iccevaṃ   vi machasaṃ syā 
    Īsānaṃ rukkhamāvahati   machasaṃ    Īsa   syā  
  
                    
      Taṃ co vadāmi bhaddaṃ    vo yāvantettha samāgatā  
 Sammodatha māvivadittha mā hotha issaphandanā  
  
      Sāmaggimeva sikkhetha buddhehetaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ  
 Sāmaggirato    dhammaṭṭho yogakkhemā na dhaṃsatiti  
   Endanajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Idheva haṃsa nipata sipiyaṃ me tava dasasnaṃ  
 Issarosi anuppanto yaṃ idhatthi pavedaya  
  
                    
      Savaṇena cekassa    piyā bhavanti 
 Disvā panekassa viyeti    chando  
 Disvā ca sutvā ca piyā bhavanti  
 Kaccinnu    me piyyasi dassanena  
  
      Samaṇena piyo mesi bhiyyo cāgamma dassanaṃ  
 Evaṃ piyadassano samāno vasa haṃsa mama santike 
  
      Vaseyyāma tavāgāre niccaṃ sakkatapujitā  
 Matto ca ekadā vajā    haṃsarājaṃ pacantu me  
  
                    
      Dhiratthu taṃ antapānaṃ yamme piyataraṃ tayā  
 Na cāpi majjaṃ pāyāmi yāva me vacchasi ghare  
  
      Suvijānaṃ sigālānaṃ sakuntānañca vassitaṃ  
 Manussavassitaṃ rāja dubbijānataraṃ tato  
  
      Api ce maññati poso ñāti mitto sakhāti vā  
 Yo    pubbe sumano hutvā pacchā sampajjate diso  
  
      Yasmiṃ mano nivisati avidūre sabhāpi so    
 Santikepi hi so dūre yasmā vivasate mano  
  
   Bhaddante   machasaṃ   Sāmagya   machasaṃ   Ekassa   syā nekassa   machasaṃ   
 Viheti   vi vineti   machasaṃ syā 
   Kacci nu me piyasi   syā   Vajje   machasaṃ vajjaṃ   syā 
   So   machasaṃ   Yo   vi  
                    
      Antopi so    hoti pasanna citto 
 Pāraṃ samuddassa pasannacittā  
 Antopi yo hoti paduṭṭhavitto 
 Pāraṃ samuddassa paduṭṭacitto  
  
      Saṃvasantāpi vivasanti ye disā    te rathesabha  
 Ārā santo saṃvasanti    manasā raṭṭhavaḍḍhana  
  
      Aticiraṃ nivāsena piyo bhavati appiyo  
 Āmanta kho taṃ gacchāma    purā te homa    appiyā    
  
                    
      Evaṃ ce yācamānānaṃ añjaliṃ nāvakhujjhasi  
 Parivārakānaṃ sattānaṃ vacanaṃ na karosi no  
 Evaṃ taṃ abhiyācāma puna kayirāsi pariyāyaṃ  
  
      Evaṃ ce no viharataṃ antarāyo na hessati  
 Tuyhaṃ cāpi mahārāja mayhaṃ vā raṭṭhavaḍḍhana    
 Appevanāma passema    ahorattānamaccayeti  
   Javanahaṃsajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Na te kaṭṭhāni bhinnāni na te udakamāhataṃ  
 Aggipi te na hāsito    kinnu mandeva jhāyasi  
  
      Na ussabhe vane vatthuṃ kassapāmantayāmi taṃ  
 Dukkho vāso araññasmiṃ eṭṭhaṃ icchāmi gantave  
  
      Yathā ahaṃ ito gantvā yasmiṃ janapade vasaṃ  
 Ācāraṃ buhme     sikkheyyaṃ taṃ dhammaṃ anusāsa maṃ  
  
                    
      Sace araññaṃ hitvāna manamulaphalāni ca  
 Raṭṭhe rocayase vāsaṃ taṃ dhammaṃ nisāmehi me  
  
   Ce   syā   Tādisā   machasaṃ   Ārādhitā saṃvasantimachasaṃ   Gaccāmi   syā   Hotha 
   machasaṃ syā   Appiyo   syā   Eṭṭhavaddana   Pamusse   machasaṃ   Hāpito   
 machasaṃ 
    Ācāraṃ brahmaṃ   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Visaṃ mā patisevittho papātaṃ parivajjaya  
 Paṅke    ca mā visidittho    yatto āsivise    care 
  
      Kinnu visaṃ papāto vā paṅko vā brahmacārinaṃ  
 Kaṃ tvaṃ āsivisaṃ brūhi tamme akkhāhi pucchito  
  
      Āsavo tāta lokasmiṃ surā nāma pavuccati  
 Manuñāñā    surahi vaggu madhukhudadarasupamā    
 Visaṃ tadāhu ariyā brahmacariyassa nārada  
  
      Itthiyo tāta lokasmiṃ pamattaṃ pamathenati tā  
 Haranti yuvino    cittaṃ tulabhaṭṭaṃva    māḷuto 
 Papāto eso akkhāto brahmacariyassa nārada  
  
      Lābho siloko sakkāro pujā parakulesu ca  
 Paṅko eso    akkhāto brahmacariyassa nārada  
  
      Sasatthā    tāta rājāno āvasanti mahiṃ imaṃ  
 Te tāsise manussinde mahante tāta nārada  
  
                    
      Issarānaṃ adhipatinaṃ na tesaṃ pādato care  
 Āsiviso so akkāto brahmacariyassa nārada  
  
      Bhattattho     bhattakāle yaṃ yaṃ gehaṃ upasaṅkame  
 Yadettha kusalaṃ jaññā tattha ghāsesanaṃ care  
  
      Pavisitvā parakulaṃ pānatthaṃ     bhojanāya vā  
 Mitaṃ khāde mitaṃ bhuñeja na ca rupe manaṃ kare  
  
      Goṭṭhaṃ     majjaṃ kirāsañca     sabhāni kiraṇāni ca  
 Ārakā parivajjeti yāniva     visamaṃ pathanti  
   Cullanāradajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Dute te brahme     pāhesiṃ gaṅgātirasmiṃ jhāyato  
 Tesaṃ puṭṭho na vyākāsi     dukkhaṃ guhaṃ matannu te  
  
   Paṅko   vi machasaṃ   Mahanatā   machaṣaṃ syā   Visiyittho   machasaṃ    Bhattatthe 
   machasaṃ   Cāsivise   vi machasaṃ    Pānattho   vi   Manuñño   machasaṃ    
 Guṭṭhaṃ   syā   Sādukhuddarasupamo   machasaṃ    Kirāṭañca   machasaṃ   Yatino   
 machasaṃ munino   syā    Yāniṃva   machasaṃ yāni va  vi   Kulaṃ   machasaṃ tulaṃ   
 syā    Brāhmaṇa   machasaṃ   Eso ca   machasaṃ    Byākāsi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Sace te dukkhaṃ uppajje kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhana  
 Mā kho no    tassa akkhāhi yo taṃ dukkhā na mocaye  
  
      Yo tassa dukkhajātassa ekantaṃ api bhāsato  
 Vippamoceyya dhammena kāmaṃ tassa pavedaye  
  
      Suvijānaṃ sigālānaṃ sakuntānañca    vassitaṃ 
 Manussavassitaṃ rāja dubbijānataraṃ tato  
  
                    
      Api ce maññati poso ñāti mitto sakhāti vā  
 Yo pubbe sumano hutvā pacchā sampajjate diso  
  
      Yo antano addhamanānupuṭṭho 
 Pavedaye jantu akālarūpe  
 Ānandino    tassa bhavannamittā    
  Hitesino tassa dukhi    bhavanti  
  
      Kālañca ñatvāna tatāvidhassa 
 Medhāvinaṃ ekamanaṃ viditvā  
 Akkheya tippāni parassa dhīro 
 Saṇhaṃ giraṃ atthavatiṃ pamuñce  
  
      Sace ca jaññā avisayhamattano 
 Nāyaṃ niti    mayhasukhāgamāya  
 Ekopi tippāni    saheyya dhīro  
 Saccaṃ hirottappamapekkhamāno  
  
                    
      Ahaṃ aṭṭhāni vicaranto nigame rājadhāniyo    
 Bhikkhamāno mahārāja ācariyassa    dhanatthiko  
  
      Gahapati rājapurise mahāsāle ca brāhmaṇe  
 Alatthaṃ     satta nikkhāni suvaṇaṇassa janādhipa 
 Te me naṭṭhā mahārāja tasmā socāmahaṃ bhusaṃ  
  
      Purisā te mahārāja manasā anuvicintitā 
 Nālaṃ dukkhā pamocetuṃ tasmā tesaṃ na vyāhariṃ 
  
      Tvaṃ ca kho me mahārāja manasā anuvicittito  
 Alaṃ dukkhā pamocetuṃ tasmā tuyhaṃ pavedayiṃ  
  
      Tassādisi pasannatto     kāsinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhano  
 Jātarūpamaye nikkhe suvaṇaṇassa catuddasātita 
   Dutajātakaṃ  
  
   Naṃ   machasaṃ   Sakuṇañca   machasaṃ   Anandino   machasaṃ syā   Bhananati 
 mitatā   machasaṃ syā   Dukkhi   machasaṃ syā   Kālaṃ sehi mayhaṃ   machasaṃ natehi 
 mahyaṃ   syā   Ekova tibbāti   machasaṃ ekova   vi   Rājaṭṭhāniyo   machasaṃ   Ācariya 
   machasaṃ    Alaḍaṃ   machasaṃ    Pasannavittomachasaṃ syā  
  
                     
                    
      Rājā kāliṅgo    cakkavatati 
 Dhammena paṭhavimanusāsaṃ  
 Agamā    bodhisamipaṃ 
 Nāgena mahānubhāvena  
  
      Kāliṅgo bhāradvājo 
 Rājānaṃ kāliṅgaṃ samaṇakolaññaṃ  
 Cakkaṃ vattayato pariggahetvā 
 Pañajali idamavoca    
  
      Paccoroha mahārāja 
 Bhumibhāgo yathā samanugito    
 Idha anadhivarā bududhā 
 Abhisambuddhā virocanti  
  
      Padakkhiṇato āvaṭṭā    
 Tiṇalatā asmiṃ bhumibhāgasamiṃ  
 Puthuviyā ayaṃ    maṇḍo 
 Iti no sutaṃ mahārāja    
  
      Sāgarapariyantāya 
 Mediniyā sabbabhūtadharaṇiyā  
 Puthuviyā ayaṃ maṇḍo 
 Orohitvā namo karohi  
  
      Ye te bhavanti nāgā 
 Abhijātā    mātito ca pitito ca  
 Ettāvatā padesaṃ 
 Te nāgā nevamupayanti 
  
      Abhijato te nāgo  
 Kāmaṃ pesehi kuñajaraṃ dantiṃ  
 Ettāvatā padeso 
 Sakkā nāgena mupagantuṃ    
  
   Rājā kālaṃṅgā   machasaṃ vi   Agamāsi   machasaṃ syā 
   Manusāsi   syā   Samanuggaho   machasaṃ   Āvattā   vi   Paṭhaviyā ayaṃ   syā 
 paṭhaviyaṃ nābhiyaṃ athavi sāya   machasaṃ   Iti no sutaṃ mante mahāraja   machasaṃ   
 Abhijātā ca tuñajarā   machasaṃ   Ettavatā padesoca na sakkā nāgena mupagantaṃ   
 machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Taṃ sutvā rājā kāliṅgā 
 Veyyañajanikavaco    nisāvetvā 
 Saṃpesesi nāgaṃ 
 Ñassāma    mayaṃ yathā idaṃ vacanaṃ  
  
      Saṃpesito ca raññā 
 Nāgo koñco ca abhinaditvāna  
 Paṭisakakitvā nisīdi 
 Garubhāraṃ asahamano  
  
                    
      Kāliṅgohāradvājo 
 Nāgaṃ khīṇāyukaṃ viditvāna  
 Rājānaṃ kāliṅgaṃ 
 Taramano ajjhabhāsittha Aññaṃ saṅkama nāgaṃ nāgo ṇīṇāyuko mabhārāja  
  
                    
      Taṃ sutvā kāliṅgo taramāno 
 Saṅkami nāgaṃ saṅkante ca rañño  
 Nāgo tattheva pati bhumyā 
 Veyyañajanikavaco yathā tathā ahu nāgo  
  
      Kāliṅgabhāradvājaṃ 
 Kāliṅgo brāhmaṇaṃ idamamoca   tvamevāsi sambuddho 
 Sabbaññu sabbadassāvi  
  
      Taṃ vacanaṃ anadhivāsento 
 Kāliṅgo brāhmaṇo idamavoca  
 Veyyañajanikā hi mayaṃ 
 Buddhā sabbaññunova mahārāja 
  
      Sabbaññu sabbavidu ca 
 Buddhā na lakkhane jānanti   
 Āgamabalasāhi mayaṃ 
 Buddhā sabbaṃ pajānanti  
  
   Veyyañchaniya   vi   Usasāma   machasaṃ uyyāma   syā 
   Patito   vi machasaṃ   Etadavoca   machasaṃ   na anadhivāsenetā kāliṅgo brāhmaṇo   
 syā idamavoca   machasaṃ taṃ anadhivāso kaliṅgaṃ brāhmaṇo  
  
                    
                    
      Mahāyitvāna    sambodhiṃ 
 Nānā turiyehi vajjamānehi  
 Mālāgandhavilepanaṃ    
 Āharitvā pākāraparikkhepaṃ kāresi  
  
      Saṭṭhavāhasahassānaṃ pupphānaṃ sannipātayi  
 Pujesi rājā kāliṅgo bodhimaṇḍavaruttameti  
   Kāliṅgabodhijātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Akittiṃ disvāna sammantaṃ sakko bhūtapati bravi  
 Kimatthiyaṃ mahābuhme eko sammasi ghammani  
  
                    
      Dukkho punabbhavo sakka sarīrassa ca bhedanaṃ  
 Sammebhamararaṇaṃ dukkhaṃ tasmā sammāmi vāsava  
  
      Etasmiṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Varaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñci manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakaka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Yena putte ca dāre ca dhaṇadhaññaṃ piyāni ca 
 Laddhā narā na tappanti so lobho namayi mase  
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite varaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñci 
 manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakaka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Khettaṃ vatthuṃ hiraññañca gavāssa dāsaporisaṃ  
 Yena jātena jiyanta so doso na mayi mase  
  
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite varaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñci 
 manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakaka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Bālaṃ na passe na suṇe na ca bālena saṃvase  
 Bālena allāpasallāpaṃ na kare na ca rocaye  
  
   Pasaṃsitvāna   syā   Mālāvilepanaṃ abiharitvā  machasaṃ syā 
   Gavassaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Kinnu te akaraṃ bālo vada kassapa kāraṇaṃ  
 Kena kassapa bālassa dassanaṃ nābhikaṅkhasi  
  
      Anayaṃ nati dummedho adhurāyaṃ niyuñajati  
 Dunnayo seyyaso hoti sammāvutto pakuppati 
 Vinayaṃ so na jānāti sādhu tassa adassanaṃ  
  
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite  
 Varaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñca manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Dhiraṃ passe suṇe dhiraṃ dhirena saha saṃvase  
 Dhirena alalāpasallāpaṃ taṃ kare taṃ ca rocaye  
      Kinnu te akaraṃ dhīro vada kassapa kāraṇaṃ  
 Kena kassapa dhirassa dassanaṃ abhikaṅkhasi  
  
      Nayaṃ nayati medhāvi adhurāyaṃ na yuñajati  
 Sunayo seyyaso hoti sammāvutto va pakuppati 
 Vinayaṃ so pajānāti sādhu tena samāgamo  
  
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite  
 Varaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñca manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Tato ratyā vivasane    suriyassuggamanaṃ pati  
 Dibbā bhakkhā pātubhaveyyuṃ silavanto ca yācakā  
      Dadato ca me na khiyetha datvā nānutapeyyahaṃ  
 Dadaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñci manasicchisi  
      Etasmiṃ te sulapite patirūpe subhāsite  
 Varaṃ kassapa te dammi yaṃ kiñca manasicchasi  
  
      Varaṃ ce me ado sakka sabbabhūtānamissara  
 Na maṃ puna upeyyāsi etaṃ sakka maraṃ vare  
  
   Vivasāne   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Bahuhi vattacariyāhi narā ca atha nāriyo  
 Dassanaṃ abhikaṅkhanti kinnu me dassane bhayaṃ  
  
      Taṃ tādisaṃ devavaṇṇaṃ sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ  
 Disvā tapo pamajjeyyaṃ    etaṃ te dassane bhayanti  
   Akittijātakaṃ    
  
                    
      Ahameva dubbhāsitaṃ bhāsi bālo 
 Bhoko va araññe ahimavha yānā    
 Takkāriye sobbhamimaṃ    patāmi 
 Na kireva sādhu ativelabhāṇi  
  
                    
      Pappoti macco ativelabhāṇi 
 Bandhaṃ vadhaṃ sokapariddavañca  
 Attānaṃ yeva    garahāsi etto    
 Ācera yaṃ taṃ nikhaṇanti    sobbhe  
  
                    
      Kimevāhaṃ tuṇḍila manupucchiṃ    
 Kireyya    saṃ bhātaraṃ kāḷikāyaṃ      
 Naggovahaṃ vatthayaguñca jino
