 Ayamipi attho bahutādisova  
  
                    
      Yo yujjhamānānaṃ ayujjhamāno 
 Meṇḍantaraṃ accupati kuliṅgo  
 So piṃsito meṇḍasirehi tattha 
 Ayampi attho bahutādisova  
  
                    
      Caturo janā potthakaṃ aggahesuṃ 
 Ekañca posaṃ anurakkhamānā 
 Sabbeva te bhinnasirā sayiṃsu 
 Ayampi attho bahutādisova  
  
      Ajā yathā veḷugumbasmiṃ baddhā 
 Avekkhipanti asimajjhagañaji     
 Teneva tassā galakāvakantaṃ     
 Ayampi attho bahutādisova  
  
   Pamājjayya   machasaṃ   Ācariyataṃ nikkhananti   machasaṃ syā   Akatti jātakaṃ   
 machasaṃ   Mānupaccheyyaṃ   vi machasaṃ 
   Syavhāyamāno   machasaṃ   Kareyyāsaṃ   syā kāme   machasaṃ   Sobbhamhi ahaṃ   
 machasaṃ    Kalikāyya   machasaṃ kālikāya   syā   Attanāmeva   machasaṃ    
 Ādikajjhagañachaṃ   vi machasaṃ syā   Ettha   machasaṃ    Galakaṃ vikattā   syā 
 vikantuṃ   machasaṃ  gilayā katatuṃ   machasaṃ   
                    
                    
      Nayime    devā napi    gandhabbaputtā  
 Migā ime atthavasāhatā ime    
 Ekañca naṃ sāyamāse pacantu  
 Ekañca puna pātarāse    pacantaa  
  
      Sataṃ sahassānaṃ dubbhāsitānaṃ    
 Kalampi nāgghanti subhāsitassa  
 Dubbhāsitaṃ saṅkamāno kileso 
 Tasmā tuṇhi kimpuraso na bālyā  
  
                    
      Yā mesā vyākāsi pamuñcathetaṃ  
 Giriñca    naṃ himavantaṃ nayantu  
 Imañca kho dentu mahānasāya 
 Pātova naṃ pātarāse vacantu  
  
      Pajjunnanāthā pasavo pasunāthā ayaṃ pajā  
 Tvaṃ nāthosmi mahārāja ambhanāthā mama bhariyā    
 Cinnamaññataraṃ ñatvā mutetā geccheyya pabbataṃ  
  
      Na ce nindā suparivajjayetha 
 Nānā janā sevitabbā janinda  
 Yeneva eko labhate pasaṃsaṃ 
 Teneva añño labhate ninditāraṃ  
  
                    
      Sabbo loko paricittona acitto    
 Sabbo loko vintavāsambhi citte  
 Paccekacittā puthusabbasattā 
 Kassidha cittassa vasena vattati  
  
      Tuṇhi ahu kimpuriso sabhariyo 
 Yodāni vyākāsi bhayassa hito  
 Sodāni mutto sukhito ārogo 
 Vācā kirevatthavati narānanti  
   Takkāriyajātakaṃ 
  
   Imena   machasaṃ   Nāpi   syā machasaṃ   Atthavasaṃgatā me   machasaṃ   
 Punappātarāse   machasaṃ syā   Satasabhassāni dubhāsitāni   machasaṃ   Giravaraṃ   
 machasaṃ   Nāthohaṃ bhariyāya me   machasaṃ   Atacitto   machasaṃ  
  
                    
                    
      Tassa gāmacaraṃ dammi nāriyo ca alaṃkatā ko me taṃ migamakkhāti migānaṃ 
 migamuttamaṃ  
  
      Mayhaṃ gāmavaraṃ dehi nāriyo ca alaṅkatā  
 Ahaṃ te migamakkhissaṃ migānaṃ migamuttamaṃ  
  
                    
      Etasmiṃ vanasaṇḍasmiṃ ambā sālā ca pupaphitā 
 Indagopakakasaṃchantā ettheso tiṭṭhati migo  
  
      Dhanuṃ adejjhaṃ    katvāna usuṃ sandhāyupāgami    
 Migo ca disvā rājānaṃ durato ajjhabhāsatha  
  
      Āgamehi mahārāja mā maṃ vijjhi rathesabha  
 Ko nu te idamakkhāsi    ettheso tiṭṭhati migo  
  
                    
      Esa pāpacaro poso samma tiṭṭhati ārakā  
 So hi me idamakkhāsi ettheso tiṭṭhati migo  
  
      Saccaṃ kireva māhaṃsu narā ekacciyā idha  
 Kaṭṭhaṃ vipalāvitaṃ    seyyo natvevekacciyo naro  
  
                    
      Kinnu rurū garahasi migānaṃ 
 Kiṃ pakkhinaṃ kiṃ pana mānusānaṃ  
 Bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati napparūpaṃ 
 Sutvānaṃ taṃ mānusiṃ bhāsamānaṃ  
  
      Yamuddhariṃ vahane    vuyhamānaṃ 
 Mahodake salile sighasote  
 Tato nidānaṃ bhayamāgataṃ mama 
 Dukkho bhave rāja asabbhisaṅgamo  
  
      Sohaṃ catuppannamidaṃ vihaṅgamaṃ 
 Tanu cchidaṃ bhadaye ossajāmi  
 Hanāmi mittadadumakiccakāriṃ 
 Yo tādisaṃ kammakataṃ na jāne  
  
   Dhanu sarajjuṃ   machasaṃ   Sannayhupāgamiṃ   machasaṃ   Idhaṃ   machasaṃ   
 Kaṭṭhaṃ nipāvataṃ   syā kaṭṭha nipalavitaṃ   machasaṃ   Vāhane   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
                    
      Dhirassa bālassa bhave janinda 
 Santo vadhaṃ nappasaṃsanti jātu  
 Kāmaṃ gharaṃ gacchatu pāpadhammo 
 Yañcassa bhaṭṭhaṃ tadetassa dehi 
 Ahañca te kāmakaro bhavāmi  
  
      Addhā rurū aññataro sataṃ se    
 Yo dubbhato mānusassa na dubbhi    
 Tāmaṃ gharaṃ gacchatu pāpadhammo 
 Yañcassa bhaṭṭhaṃ tadetassa dammi 
 Ahañca te kāmacāraṃ    dadāmi  
  
      Suvijānaṃ sigālānaṃ sakuntānañca vassitaṃ  
 Manussavassitaṃ rāja dubbijānataraṃ tato  
  
      Api ce maññati poso ñāti mitto sakhāti vā  
 Yo pubbe sumano hutvā pacchā sampajjate diso 
  
                    
      Samāgatā jānapadā    negamā ca samāgatā  
 Migā    dhaññāni khādanti taṃ devo paṭisedhatu    
  
      Kāmaṃ janapado    māsi raṭṭhaṃvāpi vinassatu  
 Natvevāhaṃ rurūṃ dubbhe datvā abhayadakkhīṇaṃ  
  
      Mā me janapado āsi raṭṭhañcapi vinassatu  
 Natveva    miga rājassa varaṃ datvā musā bhaṇeti  
   Rūrumigajātakaṃ  
                    
  
      Āsiṃsetheva    puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ yathā icchiṃ tathā ahu  
  
      Āsiṃsetheva puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 Passāmi vohaṃ antānaṃ udakā thalamubbhataṃ  
      Vāyametheva     puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 Passāmi vohaṃ antānaṃ yathā icchiṃ tathā ahu 
  
   Sataṃ so   machasaṃ   Paṭisedhetu   machasaṃ 
   Dubhato   vi dubbhito   syā   Janappado   machasaṃ 
   Gāmavaraṃ   machasaṃ syā   Natvevāhaṃ   vi 
   Janappadā   machasaṃ   Āsasetheva   machasaṃ 
   Migāsassāni   machasaṃ    Vāyāmetheva   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Vāyametheva puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 Passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ udakā thalamubbhataṃ  
  
                    
      Dukkhupinatopi nāro sapañño 
 Āsaṃ na chindeyya sukhāgamāya  
 Bahuhi phassā ahitā hitā ca 
 Avitakkitā maccumupabbajatti  
  
      Avittitampi bhavati cintitampi vinassati  
 Nahi vintāmayā bhogā itthiyā purisassa vā  
  
                    
      Sarabhaṃ giriduggasmiṃ yaṃ tvaṃ anusari pure  
 Alinacittassa tuvaṃ vikkannamanujivasi  
  
      Yo taṃ viduggā narakā samuddhari 
 Silāya yoggaṃ sarabho karitvā  
 Dukkhupanitaṃ maccumukhā pamocayi 
 Alinacintaṃ tamigaṃ vadesi  
  
      Tuvaṃ nu tattheva tadā ahosi 
 Udāhu te koci naṃ etadakkha  
 Vivantacchaddo    nusi sabbadassi 
 Ñāṇannu te brāhmaṇa bhiṃsarūpaṃ  
  
                    
      Na cevahaṃ tattha tadā ahosiṃ 
 Na cāpi me koci naṃ etadakkhā  
 Gāthāpadānañca subhāsitānaṃ 
 Atthaṃ tadā nenti janinda dhīrā  
  
      Ādāya pattiṃ paraviriyaghātiṃ 
 Cāpe saraṃ kiṃ vicikicchase tuvaṃ  
 Nuṇeṇā    saro sarabhaṃ hantu khippaṃ 
 Annaṃ hi etaṃ varapañña rañño  
  
                    
      Addhā pajānāmi ahampi etaṃ 
 Annaṃ migo brāhmaṇa khantiyassa  
 Pubbe katañca apacāyamāno 
 Tasmā migaṃ sarabhaṃ no hanāmi  
  
   Vivaṭṭacchedo   machasaṃ vivaṭacchado   syā   Nunto   vi  
  
                    
      Neso migo mahārāja asureso    disampati  
 Etaṃ hantvā manussinda bhavassu amarādhipo  
  
      Saveva rāja    vicikicchase tuvaṃ 
 Hantuṃ migaṃ sarabhaṃ sahāyakaṃ me 
 Sapunnadāro naraviriyaseṭṭha    
 Gantā tuvaṃ vetaraṇiṃ    yamassa  
  
      Kāmaṃ ahaṃ jānapadā ca sabbe 
 Puttā ca dārā ca sahāyasaṅghā  
 Gacchemu naṃ vetaraṇiṃ yamassa 
 Natteva hañño    yo mamapāṇadassa    
  
                    
      Ayaṃ migo kicchagatassa mayhaṃ 
 Ekassa kattā vivanasmiṃ ghore 
 Taṃ tādisaṃ pubbakiccaṃ saranto 
 Jānaṃ mahābuhme kathaṃ haneyyaṃ  
  
      Mittābhīrādhi    cirameva jiva 
 Rajjaṃ imaṃ dhammaguṇe pasāsa    
 Nārigaṇehi parivārayanto 
 Modassu raṭṭhe tidiveva vāsavo  
  
      Akkodhano niccapasannacitto 
 Sabbātithiyācayogo bhavitvā    
 Datvā ca bhutvā ca yathānubhāvaṃ 
 Anindito saggamupehi ṭhānanti  
    Sarabhamigajātakaṃ  
  
 Terasakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Carakamba     kuṭṭhārisahaṃvaro 
 Atha raññasmiṃ dutakapañcako 
 Atha khodhi akittisutattarinā 
 Atha rūrumigena pārāsarehoti  
  
   Asuro so   vi   Rājā   mi mi   Naraviraseṭṭhaṃmachasaṃ syā   Vattaraṇi   machasaṃ   
 Bhañña   machasaṃ syā   Mama pāṇa   machasaṃ   Mittābhidhirā   machasaṃ   
 Rajajampivassa paṇepasaṃsa   machasaṃ   Sabbātithi pāhutake karitvā   syā sabbatithi 
 yāvayoge viditvā   machasaṃ    Caramamba  syā  
  
                     
                    
      Sampannaṃ sālikedāraṃ suvā bhuñjanti kosiya  
 Paṭivedemi te brahme na na    vāretu mussahe 
  
      Eko ca tattha sakuṇo so tesaṃ    sabbasundaro  
 Bhutvā sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ tuṇḍenādāya gacchati  
      Oḍḍentu    vāḷapāsāni yathā bajjhetha so dijo  
 Jivañca naṃ gahetvāna ānayetha mamantike  
  
                    
      Ete bhutvā vivitvā ca pakkamanti vihaṃgamā  
 Eko baddhosmi pāsena kiṃ pāpaṃ pakatammayā  
  
      Udaraṃ nūna aññesaṃ suva accodaraṃ tava  
 Bhutvā sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ tuṇḍenādāya gaccasi  
  
      Koṭṭhannu tattha puresi suva verannu te mayā 
 Puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kuhiṃ sāliṃ nidhiyasi  
  
                    
      Na me ceraṃ tayā saddhiṃ koṭṭho mayhaṃ na vijjati  
 Iṇaṃ muñcāmiṇaṃdammi sampatto koṭisimbaliṃ    
 Nidimpi tattha nidahāmi evaṃ jānāhi kosiya  
  
      Kisisaṃ te iṇadānaṃ iṇamokkho ca kidiso  
 Nidhiṃ    nidhānaṃ akkhāhi atha pāsā pamokkhasi  
  
      Ajātapakkhā taruṇā puttakā mayha    kosiya  
 Te maṃ bhatā bharissanti tasmā tesaṃ iṇaṃ dade  
  
      Mātā pitā ca me vuddhā jiṇaṇakā gatayobbanā  
 Tesaṃ tuṇḍena bhātuna muñce pubbe kataṃ    iṇaṃ  
  
      Aññepi tattha sakuṇā khiṇapakkhā sudubbalā  
 Tesaṃ puññatthiko dammi taṃ nidhiṃ āhu paṇḍitā  
  
   Nane   machasaṃ nate   syā   Yo nesaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Ujjhantu   machasaṃ syā   
 Koṭasimabali   machasaṃ 
   Nidhinidhāna makkhāhi   machasaṃ   Mayhaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Pubbakataṃ   vi machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Edisaṃ    me iṇadānaṃ iṇamokkho me ediso  
 Nidhiṃ nidhānaṃ akkhātaṃ    evaṃ jānāhi kosiya  
  
      Bhaddako vanayaṃ    pakkhī dvijo paramadhammiko  
 Ekaccesu manussesu ayaṃ dhammo na vijjati  
  
                    
      Bhuñja sāliṃ yathākāmaṃ saha sabbehi ñātihi  
 Punāpi suva passemu piyaṃ me tava dassanaṃ  
  
      Bhuttañca pitañca tavassamambhi 
 Rativa no kosiya te sakāse  
 Nikkhintadaṇḍesu dadāhi dānaṃ  
 Jiṇeṇava mātāpitaro bharassu  
  
      Lakkhi vata me udapādi ajja 
 Yo addasāsiṃ    pavaraṃ dijānaṃ  
 Suvassa sutvāna subhāsitāni 
 Kāhāmi puññāni anappakāni  
  
                    
      So kosiyo attamano udaggo 
 Antañca pānañcabhisaṅkharitvā    
 Annena pānena pasannacitto 
 Santappayi samaṇe brāhmaṇecāti  
   Sālikedārajātakaṃ    
  
                    
      Upaniyatidaṃ maññe 
 Cande lohitamadena majjāmi  
 Vijahāmi jivataṃ pāṇā 
 Me cande nirujjhanti    
  
      Osadhi me dukkhaṃ me 
 Hadayaṃ me dayhate nitammāmi  
 Tava candiyā socantiyā 
 Na naṃ aññehi sokehi  
  
   Īdisaṃ   machasaṃ   Nidhinidhānamakkhāmi   machasaṃ   Vatāyaṃ   syā vi   Yohaṃ 
 adassaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Haritvā   vi kari   machasaṃ   Kerajātakaṃ   machasaṃ   
 Upaniyyatidaṃ maññe   cande lohita maddane ajja jahāmi jīvita   pāṇā me vande 
 nirāpajhanti   machasaṃ ajjāsi vijahāmi jīvitaṃ Syā  
  
                    
      Tiṇamiva vanamiva miyyāmi    
 Nadi aparipuṇaṇiyāva sussāmi  
 Tava candiyā sovantiyā 
 Na naṃ aññehi sokekahi  
  
      Vassaṃva sare pāde 
 Imāni massuni vattare mayhaṃ  
 Tava candiyā socantiyā 
 Na naṃ aññehi sokehi  
                    
      Pāposi kho rājaputta 
 Yo me icchitapatiṃ varākiyā  
 Vijjhi vanamulasmiṃ 
 So yaṃ viddho chamā seti  
  
      Imaṃ mayhaṃ bhadayasokaṃ 
 Paṭimuñcatu rājaputta tava mātā  
 Yo mayhaṃ bhadayasoko 
 Kimpurisaṃ avekkhamānāya  
  
      Imaṃ mayhaṃ bhadayasokaṃ 
 Paṭimuñcatu rājaputta tava jātā  
 Yo mayhaṃ bhadayasoko 
 Kimpurisaṃ avekkhamānāya  
  
      Mā ca putte    mā ca patiṃ 
 Addakkhi rājaputta tava mātā  
 Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi 
 Adūsakaṃ    mayhakāmāhi  
  
      Mā ca putte mā ca patiṃ     
 Addakkhi rājaputta tava jātā  
 Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi 
 Adūsakaṃ mayhakāmāhi    
  
      Mā tuvaṃ cande rujji    
 Mā soci manatimiramattikkhi  
 Mama tvaṃ hohisi bhariyā 
 Rājakule pujitā nārī    
  
   Milāyāmi   machasaṃ   Māva puttaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Avidusakaṃ   mi   Mayhaṃ 
 kāmā vi mayhaṃkāmāhi   machasaṃ   Rodi   machasaṃ   Nārihi   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Apinunahaṃ    marissaṃ 
 Nacapanāhaṃ    rājaputta tava hessaṃ 
 Yo kimpurisaṃ avadhi 
 Adūsakaṃ mayhakāmāhi  
  
      Api bhīruke apijīvitukāmike 
 Kimpurisi gaccha himavannaṃ  
 Tālissatagarabhojane    
 Araññe taṃ migā ramissanti  
  
      Te pabbatā tāva kandarā 
 Tā ca giriguhāyo  
 Tattha    taṃ apassanti 
 Kiṃpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ    
  
      Te paṇṇasatthatā ramaṇiyā  
 Vāḷamigehi anuciṇaṇā  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kiṃpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Te pupphasatthāramaṇiyā  
 Vāḷamigehi anuciṇaṇā  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kiṃpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
                    
      Acchā samanti girivaranadiyo     
 Kusumābhikiṇaṇasotāyo  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kiṃpurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Nilāni himavato  
 Pabbatassa kuṭāni dassaneyyāna  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Pitāni himavato  
 Pabbatassa kuṭāni dassaneyyāna  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
   Syā vi nunāhaṃ   machasaṃ   Kāhaṃ   machasaṃ   Tālisa taggarabhojanā   machasaṃ Syā 
   Tattheva   vi machasaṃ   Kasasaṃ   vi machaṃ   Hirivana nadiyo   machasaṃ vi  
  
                    
      Tambāni himavato  
 Pabbatassa kuṭāni dassaneyyāna  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Tuṅgāni himavato  
 Pabbatassa kuṭāni dassaneyyāna  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Setāni himavato  
 Pabbatassa kuṭāni dassaneyyāna  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Citrāni himavato  
 Pabbatassa kuṭāni dassaneyyāna  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Yakkhagaṇasevite  
 Gandhamādane osadhehi sañachanne  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
      Kimpurisasevite  
 Gandhamādane osadhehi sañachanne  
 Tattha taṃ apassanti 
 Kimapurisa kathaṃ ahaṃ kāsaṃ  
  
                    
      Vande te pāde ayira brahme     
 Yo me ḍacchitapatiṃ varākiyā  
 Amatena abhisiñci  
 Samāgatasmiṃ piyatamena  
  
      Vicarāma dāni girivaranadiyo 
 Kusumābikiṇaṇasotāyo  
 Nānādumavasanāyo 
 Piyaṃvadā aññamaññassāti  
   Candakinnarajātakaṃ  
  
   Cande te ayire brahme   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Ukkā    milāvā bandhanti dīpe 
 Pajā mamaṃ    khādituṃ patthayanti  
 Mintaṃ sahāyañca vadehi    senaka 
 Ādikkha ñātivyasanaṃ dijānaṃ 
  
      Dijo dijānaṃ pavarosi pakkhi  
 Ukkusarāja    saraṇaṃ taṃ upemi  
 Pajā mama khādituṃ patthayanti 
 Luddā milāvā bhava me sukhāya  
  
      Mittaṃ sahāyañca karonti paṇḍitā 
 Kāle akāle sukamesamānā    
 Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ 
 Ariyo hi ariyassa karoti kiccaṃ  
  
                    
      Yaṃ hoti kiccaṃ anukampakena 
 Ariyassa ariyena kataṃ tavayidaṃ    
 Attānurakkhi bhava mā aḍayha 
 Lacchāma putte tayi jivamāne  
  
      Taveva    rakkhāvaraṇaṃ karonto 
 Sarīrabhedāpi na santasāmi  
 Karonti heke    sakhinaṃ sakhāro 
 Pāṇaṃ cajanti    sata     mesadhamme  
  
                    
      Sudukkaraṃ kammamakā     aṇḍajāyaṃ vihaṅgamo 
 Atthāya kuraro     putte aḍḍharatte anāgate  
  
      Cutāpi eke khalitā sakammunā  
 Mittānukampāya patiṭṭhahanti  
 Puttā mamaṭṭā gatimāgatosmi 
 Atthaṃ caretha mema cārichanta  
  
      Dhanena dhaññena ca attanāva 
 Mittaṃ sahāyañca karonti paṇḍitā  
 Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ 
 Ariyo hi ariyassa karoti kiccaṃ  
  
   Luddā   machasaṃ vi   Tameva   machasaṃ syā 
   Mama   syā   Hete   machasaṃ 
   Parehi   vi   Vajantā   machasaṃ syā 
   Ukkusa   vi    Sataṃ nesa machasaṃ ākānesa vi 
   Māyayānā   vi    Kamma makāsi   machasaṃ syā 
   Tayidaṃ   machasaṃ syā    Kururo   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
                    
      Appossukko tāta tuvaṃ nisida    
 Putto pitu carati atthacariyaṃ  
 Ahaṃ carissāmi tavetamatthaṃ    
 Senayassa putte paritāyamāno  
  
      Addhā hi tāta satamesa dhammo 
 Putto pitu yaṃ caretha atthacariyaṃ  
 Appeva maṃ disvā pavaḍḍhakāyaṃ    
 Senassa putte na viheṭhayeyyuṃ    
  
                    
      Pasu manussā migaviriyaseṭṭha    
 Bhayadditā    seṭṭhamupabbajanti    
 Puttā mamaṭṭā gatimāgatosmi 
 Tvaṃ nosi rājā bhava me sukhāya  
  
      Karomi te senaka etamatthaṃ 
 Āyāma    te taṃ disataṃ vadhāya  
 Kathaṃ hi viññu pahu     sampajāno 
 Na vāyame attajanassa guttiyā  
  
                    
      Mittañca     kayirātha subhaddayañca     
 Ayirañca kayirātha sukhehi ayiro     
 Nivatthakojo va sarebhihanatvā 
 Modāma puttehi samaṅgibhūtā  
  
      Sakamittassa     kammena sahāya ssāpalāyino  
 Kujantamupakujanti     lomasā hadayaṅgamaṃ  
  
      Mittaṃ sahāyaṃ adhigamma paṇḍito 
 So bhuñjati putatapasuṃ     dhanaṃ vā  
 Ahañca puttā ca pati ca mayhaṃ 
 Mittanukampāya samaṅgibhūtā  
  
      Rājāvatā suravatā ca attho 
 Sampanna sakkhissa     bavanti hete  
 So mittavā yasavā uggatatto 
 Asmiñca     loke modati kāmakāmi  
  
   Nisīdi   machasaṃ    Bahu   machasaṃ vi 
   Taveva   machasaṃ syā vi    Mittaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Pitunaṃ care   machasaṃ    Sakāgharañca   vi 
   Pavaddhakāyaṃ pavaḍḍhakāyaṃ   machasaṃ syā vi    Yukhaṃgamaya   machasaṃ syā 
   Na heṭhayeyyuṃ   vi na heṭhapeyyuṃ machasaṃ    Sataṃ vi sakaṃ   machasaṃ   
 Viraseṭṭha   machasaṃ syā    Kujantaṃ   machasaṃ vi 
   Bhayaṭṭitā   machasaṃ syā    Mitta machasaṃ putta vi 
   Jajanti   machasaṃ    Sakhissa   machasaṃ 
   Āyāmi   machasaṃ    Asmidha   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Karaṇiyāni    mittāni daḷiddenāpi senaka  
 Passa mittānukampāya samaggambhā sañātake  
  
      Surena balavantena yo mettiṃ    kurute dijo  
 Evaṃ so sukhito hoti yathāhaṃ tvañca senakāti  
   Mahāukkusajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Kharājinā jaṭilā saṅkadantā 
 Dummukharūpā    ye me japanti    
 Kaccinnu    te mānusake payoge 
 Idaṃ vidu parimuttā apāyā  
  
                    
      Pāpāni kammāni karotha    rāja 
 Bahussuto ce na careyya dhammaṃ  
 Sahasasavedāpi na taṃ paṭicca 
 Dukkhā pamucce caraṇaṃ apatvā  
  
      Sahassavedopi na taṃ paṭicca 
 Dukkhā pamucca caraṇaṃ apatvā 
 Maññāmi vedā aphalā bhavanti 
 Sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇaññeva sacacaṃ  
  
                    
      Naheva vedā aphalā bhavanti 
 Sasaṃyamaṃ caraṇaneññava saccaṃ  
 Kittiṃ    hi pappoti adhicca vede 
 Yantiṃ puṇoti    caraṇena danto  
  
      Bhaccā mātā pitā bandhu yena jāto    sayeva   so  
 Uddalako ahaṃ bhoto     sotthiyā     kulavaṃsako  
  
                    
      Kathaṃ bho brāhmaṇo hoti kathaṃ bhavati kevalī  
 Kathañca parinibbānaṃ dhammaṭṭho kinti vuccati  
  
      Niraṃ katvā aggimādāya brāhmaṇo 
 Āposijaṃ     yajamusseti yupaṃ  
 Evaṃ karo brāhmaṇo hoti khemi 
 Dhamme ṭhitaṃ tena amāpayiṃsu  
  
   Karaniyyāni   vi   Jate   machasaṃ   Yomittaṃ   machasaṃ   Dummukkharūpā syā 
 dummakkharūpāmi rummakkharūpā syā aposiñcaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Mantaṃjappanti   machasaṃ    Sva   syā 
   Kaccinnu   machasaṃ syā vi    Bhoti   machasaṃ 
   Kareyyātha syā kareyya   machasaṃ    Sotthiya   machasaṃ 
   Kittiṃ va   syā    Āposiñca   machasaṃ 
   Santipuṇāti   machasaṃ 
  
                    
      Na suddhi sevanenatthi napi    kevali brāhmaṇo  
 Na khanti napi soracca    napi so parinibbuto  
  
      Kathaṃ so brāhmaṇo hoti kathaṃ bhavati kevalī  
 Kathañca parinibbānaṃ dhammaṭṭho kinti vuccati  
  
                    
      Akkhetatabandhu    amamo nirāso 
 Nillobhapāpo bhavalobhakhiṇo  
 Evaṃ karo brāhmano hoti khemi 
 Dhamme ṭhitaṃ tena amāpayiṃsu  
  
      Khantiyā brāhmaṇā vessā saddā caṇḍāla pukkusā  
 Sabbeva soratā dantā sabbeva parinibbutā  
 Sabbesaṃ sitibhūtānaṃ atthi seyyova pāpiyo  
  
      Khantiyā brāhmaṇā vessā saddā caṇḍāla pukkusā  
 Sabbeva soratā dantā sabbeva parinibbutā  
 Sabbesaṃ sitibhūtānaṃ atthi seyyova pāpiyo  
  
      Khantiyā brāhmaṇā vessā saddā caṇḍāla pukkusā  
 Sabbeva soratā dantā sabbeva parinibbutā  
  
      Sabbesaṃ sitibhūtānaṃ natthi seyyova pāpiyo Sanaṭṭhaṃ carasi brahmaññaṃ sotthiyā 
 kulavaṃsataṃ  
  
                    
      Nānārattehi vatthehi vimānaṃ bavati chāditaṃ  
 Na tesaṃ chāyāvatthānaṃ so rāgo apanujjatha  
  
      Evameva manussesu yadā    sujjhanatati mānavā  
 Na tesaṃ jātiṃ pucchanti dhammamaññāya subbatāti  
   Uddālakajātakaṃ  
  
   Nāpi   vi   Nameva khantisoraccaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Akhetta   machasaṃ syā vi   Sadā   vi  
  
  
                    
                    
      Assaṃ gavaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ 
 Bhariyañca so idha labhataṃ manāpaṃ  
 Puttehi dārehi samaṅgi hotu 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā 
  
                    
      Mālañca so kāsikacandanañca 
 Dhāretu puttassa bahu bhavantu  
 Kāmesu tibbaṃ kurutaṃ apekkhaṃ 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      Pahūtadhañño kasimā yasassī 
 Putte gihi dhanimā sabbakāme  
 Vayaṃ apassaṃ gharamāvasātu 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      So khantiyo hotu    pasayhakāri 
 Rājābhirājā balavā yasassi  
 Sacāturantaṃ mahimāvasātu bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      So brāhmaṇo hotu avitarāgo 
 Muhuttanakkhantapathesu yutto  
 Pujetu naṃ raṭṭhapati yassi 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      Ajjhāyakaṃ sabbasamattavedaṃ    
 Tapassinaṃ maññatu sabbaloko  
 Pujentu    taṃ jānapadā samecca 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      Catussadaṃ gāmavaraṃ samiddhaṃ 
 Dinnaṃ hi bhuñjatu vāsavena  
 Avitarāgo maraṇaṃ upetu 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
                    
      So gāmaṇi hotu sahāyamajjhe 
 Na ccehi gitehi pamodamāno  
 Mā rājato vyasanamalatthaki ñca 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
   Hoti   vi   Samantavedaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Pujetu   vi  
  
                    
      Yaṃ ekarājā paṭhaviṃ vijetvā    
 Itthī sahassassa    ṭhapetu aggaṃ 
 Simannininaṃ pavarā bhavātu    
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      Isinaṃ    hi sā sabbasamāgatānaṃ 
 Bhuñejayya sāduṃ aivakampamānā  
 Carātu lābhena vikatthamānā 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
      Āvāsiko hotu mahāvihāre 
 Navakamamiko hotu kajaṅgalāyaṃ  
 Ālokasandhiṃ    divasā karotu 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
      So khajjhataṃ    pāsasatehi chamhi   
 Rammā vanā niyatu rājadhāniṃ  
 Tuttehi so bhaññatu pācanehi 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
      Alakkamāli tipukaṇaṇaviddho    
 Laṭṭhihato sappamukhaṃ upetu  
 Sakkavacabaddho    visikhaṃ    carātu 
 Bhisāni te brāhmaṇa yo ahāsā  
  
                    
      Yo ce     anaṭṭhaṃ naṭṭhanti cāha     
 Kāmeva so labhataṃ bhuñjatañca     
 Agāramajjhe maraṇaṃ upetu 
 Yo cā bhonto saṅkati kañcideva  
  
      Yadesamānā vicaranti loke 
 Iṭṭhañca kantañca bahunnametaṃ     
 Piyaṃ manuññaṃ idha jivaloke 
 Kasmā isayo nappasaṃsanti kāme 
  
   Jitvā   machasaṃ syā   Tipukaraṇā piṭṭhe   vi  
   Sahassānaṃ   machasaṃ vi   Sakacchabandho   machasaṃ 
   Bhavatu   machasaṃ   Visikaṃ   nā 
   Dāsina   machasaṃ    Ye ve   machasaṃ 
   Ālokasandi   machasaṃ    Āha   syā 
   Bajjhatu   machasaṃ    Labhatu bhuñjatu   machasaṃ syā 
   Chamabhiti ghabbattha    Bahuta   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
      Kāmesu ce ha ññare khajjhare ca 
 Kāmesu dukkhañca bhayañca jātaṃ  
 Kāmesu bhūtādhipati pamattā 
 Pāpāni kammāni karonti mohā  
  
                    
      Te pāpadhammā pasavetvā    pāpaṃ 
 Kāyassabhedā nirayaṃ vajanti  
 Ādinavaṃ kāmaguṇesu disvā 
 Tasmā isayo nappasaṃsanti kāme      Vimaṃsamāno isino bhisāni 
 Tire gahetvāna thale niṭhesiṃ  
 Suddhā apāpā isayo vasanti 
 Etāni te brāhmacāri bhisāni  
  
      Na te naṭā no pana kīḷaneyyā 
 Na bandhāvā no pana te sahāyā  
 Kismiṃ paranthambha    sahassanetta 
 Isihi tvaṃ kiḷasi devarāja  
      Ācariyo mesi pitā ca mayhaṃ 
 Esā patiṭṭhā khalitassa buhme  
 Ekāparādhaṃ khama bhuripañña 
 Na paṇḍitā kodhabalā bhavanti 
  
                    
      Suvositaṃ isinaṃ    ekarantaṃ 
 Yaṃ vāsavaṃ bhūtapatiṃ addasāma  
 Sabbeva bhonno sumanā bhavantu 
 Yaṃ buhmaṇo paccapādi bhisāni  
  
      Ahañca sāriputto ca moggallano ca kassapo  
 Anuruddho puṇeṇā ānando tadāsuṃ satta bhātaro  
  
      Bhagini uppalavaṇṇā dāsi khujjuttarā tadā  
 Citto gahapati dāso yakkho sātāgiro tadā  
  
      Pārileyyo    tadā nālo madhudho seṭṭhavānaro  
 Kāḷudāyī tadā sakko evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti  
   Bhisajātakaṃ  
  
   Pasavetva   vi   Vupatthambha   machasaṃ   Pavāsitaṃ phasinaṃ   machasaṃ   Pālileyo 
   machasaṃ syā 
  
                    
                    
      Mahesi rucino bhariyā ānitā paṭhamaṃ ahaṃ  
 Dasavasassahasasāniyaṃ maṃ surucimānayi  
  
      Sāhaṃ brāhmaṇa rājānaṃ vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ 
 Nābhijānāmi kāyena vācāya udacetasā 
 Suruciṃ atimaññittho āvivā    yadivā raho  
  
                    
      Etena saccavajjena putto uppajjataṃ ise  
 Musā me bhaṇamānāya muddhā phalatu sattadhā  
  
      Bhattumanāpassa pitā mātā cāpi suvāmino    
 Te maṃ brāhma vinetāro yāva aṭṭhaṃsu jivate  
  
      Sāhaṃ abhiṃsāratiti kāmaso dhammacāriṇi  
 Sakkaccaṃ te upaṭṭhāsiṃ rattindivamatanditā  
  
      Etena saccavajjena putto uppajjataṃ ise  
 Musā me bhaṇamānāya muddhā phalatu sattadhā  
  
      Soḷasitthisahassāni sahabhariyāni brāhmaṇa  
 Tāsu issā vā kodho vā nāhu mayhaṃ kudācanaṃ  
  
      Hitena tāsaṃ nandāmi na ca me kāci appiyā 
 Attānaṃ vānukampāmi sadā sabbā sapattiyo  
  
      Etena saccavajjena putto uppajjataṃ ise  
 Musā me bhaṇamānāya muddhā phalatu sattadhā  
  
      Dāse kammakare pesse    ye caññe anujivano  
 Posemi sahadhammena sadā pamuditindriyā  
  
      Etena saccavajjena putto uppajjataṃ ise  
 Musā me bhaṇamānāya muddhā phalatu sattadhā  
  
      Samaṇe brāhmaṇe cāpi aññe vāpi vaṇibbake  
 Tappemi antapānena sadā payatapāṇini  
  
   Avivā   machasaṃ 
   Bhattu mama sassu mātā pitā cāpicassuro syā bhattu manāpā sassu piyā mātā 
 Pitāva sassuro   machasaṃ   Yāva aṭṭhaṃsu jīvitaṃ   machasaṃ 
   Dāsakamma karā pessā   vi  
  
                    
      Etena saccavajjena putto uppajjataṃ ise  
 Musā me bhaṇamānāya muddhā phalatu sattadhā  
  
      Cātuddasi paṇaṇarasi yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhami  
 Pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāhitaṃ  
 Uposathaṃ upavasāmi sadā sīlesu saṃvutā  
  
      Etena saccavajjena putto uppajjataṃ ise  
 Musā me bhaṇamānāya muddhā phalatu sattadhā  
  
                    
      Sabbeva te dhammaguṇā rājaputti yasassini  
 Saṃvijjanti tayi bhadde ye tvaṃ kittesi attani  
  
      Khattiyo jātisampanno abhijāto yasamasmimā  
 Dhammarājā videhānaṃ putto uppajjate    tavaṃ    
  
                    
      Rummi    rajojalladharo aghe vehāsayaṃ ṭhito  
 Manuññaṃ bhāsasi    vācaṃ yaṃ mayhaṃ hadayaṅgamaṃ  
  
      Devatānusi saggamhā isivāsi    mahiddhiko  
 Kovāsi tvaṃ anuppatto attānaṃ me pavedaya  
  
      Yaṃ devasaṅghā vandatti sudhammāyaṃ    samāgatā  
 Sohaṃ sakko sahassakkho āgatosmi tavantike  
  
      Itthiyo jivalokasmiṃ yā honti samacārinī  
 Medhāvini silavati sassudevā patibbatā  
  
      Tādisāya sumedhāya suvikammāya nāriyā  
 Devā dassanamāyanti mānusiyā amānusā  
  
      Tvañca bhadde suciṇṇena pubbe sucaritena ca  
 Idha rājakule jātā sabbakāmasamiddhini  
  
      Ayañca te rājaputti ubhayattha kaṭaggaho  
 Devalokupapatti ca kitti ca idha jivite  
  
      Ciraṃ sumedhe sukhini dhammaṃ pālayamattani    
 Esāhaṃ tidivaṃ yāmi piyamme ta va dasasnanti  
   Surucijātakaṃ  
  
   Upajjajate   syā   Tava   vi   Dummi   machasaṃ syā 
   Bhāsase   machasaṃ syā   Isicāpi isivāpi   machasaṃ syā   Sudhammāya   machasaṃ 
 syā   Dhamma mattani pālaya   vi  
  
                     
                    
      Appossukkodāni tuvaṃ kapota 
 Vihaṅgama na tava bhojanattho  
 Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto 
 Kasmā bhavaṃ posathiko kapoto  
      Ahaṃ pure giddhigato kapotiyā 
 Asmiṃ padesasmiṃ ubho ramāma  
 Athaggahi sākuṇiko kapotiṃ 
 Akāmako tāya vinā ahosiṃ  
  
      Nānābhavā    vippayogena tassā 
 Manomayaṃ vedanaṃ vediyāmi    
 Tasmā ahaṃ posathaṃ    pālayāmi 
 Rāgo mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi  
  
                    
      Anujjugāmi uraga    vijivha  
 Dāṭhāvudho ghoravisosi passa  
 Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto 
 Kasmā bhavaṃ posathiko nu dīgho  
  
      Usabho ahu balavā gāmikassa 
 Calakkuku vaṇṇabalupapanto 
 Maṃ akkami taṃ kupito aḍaṃsiṃ    
 Dukkhāhituṇṇo maraṇaṃ upāgami    
  
      Tato janā nikkhamitvāna gāmā  
 Kanditvā roditvā apakkamiṃsu  
 Tasmā ahaṃ posathaṃ pālayāmi 
 Kodho mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi  
  
      Mātāna    maṃsāni bahu susāne  
 Manuññarūpaṃ tava bhojanetaṃ  
 Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto 
 Kasmā bhavaṃ posathiko sigālo  
  
   Kapoṭa   vi   Nānābhāva   syā 
   Vedayāmi   machasaṃ syā   Posatha   machasaṃ syā 
   Uraga dujivaha machasaṃ uragā dujimbhā   syā   Aṇḍajiṃ   vi 
   Upāgā   machasaṃ syā   Matānaṃ   machasaṃ vi  
   Saṅgalo   vi  
                    
      Pavissa    kucchiṃ mahato gajassa 
 Kuṇape rato hatthamaṃse pagiddho  
 Uṇho ca vāto tikhiṇā ca rasmiyo 
 Te sosayuṃ tassa karīsamaggaṃ  
  
      Kiso ca paṇḍu ca ahaṃ bhadante    
 Na me ahu nikkhamanāya maggo  
 Mahā ca megho sahasā pavassi 
 So temayi tassa karisamaggaṃ  
  
                    
      Tato ahaṃ nikakhamissaṃ bhadante 
 Cando yathā rāhumukhā pamutto  
 Tasmā ahaṃ posathaṃ pālayāmi 
 Lobho mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsi  
  
      Vammikathupasmiṃ kipillikāni 
 Nippothayanto tuvaṃ pure carāsi  
 Khudaṃ pipāsaṃ adhivāsayanto 
 Kasmā bhavaṃ posathiko nu accho  
  
      Sakaṃ niketaṃ atihilayāno    
 Atricchatāya malataṃ    agañachiṃ  
 Tato janā nikkhamitvāna gāmā 
 Kodaṇḍakena paripothayiṃsu maṃ 
  
      So bhinnasiso rubhiramakkhitaṅgo 
 Paccāgamāsiṃ sakaṃ    niketaṃ  
 Tasmā ahaṃ posathaṃ pālayāmi 
 Atricchatā mā punarāgamāsi  
  
      Yaṃ no apucchittha tuvaṃ bhadante 
 Sabbeva vyākarimbha yathāpajānaṃ    
 Mayampi pucchāma tavaṃ bhadante    
 Kasmā bhavaṃ posathikonu brahme  
  
                    
      Anupalitto mama assamambhi 
 Paccekakhuddho muhuttaṃ nisīdi  
 So maṃ avedi gatimāgatiñca 
 Nāmañca gottaṃ caraṇañca sabbaṃ  
  
   Pavisa   machasaṃ   Malalayataṃ   machasaṃ 
   Bhaddante   machasaṃ   Sasakaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Maṃsesu   machasaṃ syā   Jānanaṃ   vi 
   Atiheḷayāno   machasaṃ syā   Tuvaṃ ma baddanta   machasaṃ vi  
  
                    
      Evampahaṃ naggahe tassa pāde 
 Na cāpi naṃ mānagatena pucchiṃ  
 Tasmā ahaṃ posathaṃ pālayāmi 
 Mano mamaṃ mā punarāgamāsiti  
   Pañcuposathajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Sace hi tyāhaṃ dhanahetu gahito 
 Mā maṃ vadhi jivagāhaṃ gahetvā  
 Rañño ca maṃ samma upenti nehi 
 Maññe dhanaṃ lacchasi napparūpaṃ  
  
      Na me ayaṃ tumbhe    vadhāya ajja 
 Samāhito cāpavaro khurappo  
 Pāsañca tyāhaṃ adhipātayisasaṃ  
 Yathā sukhaṃ gacchatu morarājā  
  
      Yaṃ satta vassāni mamānubandhi 
 Rattindivaṃ khuppipāsaṃ sahanto  
 Atha kissa maṃ pāsavasupanitaṃ 
 Pamuttave icchasi bandhanasmā  
  
      Pāṇātipātā viratonusajja 
 Abhayaṃ nu te sabbababhutesu dinnaṃ  
 Yaṃ maṃ tuvaṃ pāsavasupanitaṃ  
 Pamuttave icchāsi bandhanasmā  
  
                    
      Pāṇātipātā viratassa brūhi 
 Abhayañca yo sabbabhutesu deti  
 Pucchāmi taṃ morarājetamatthaṃ 
 Ito cuto kiṃ labhate sukhaṃ so  
  
      Pāṇātipātā viratassa brūmi 
 Abhayañca yo sabbabhutesu deti  
 Diṭṭheva dhamme labhate pasaṃsaṃ 
 Saggañca so yāti sarirabhedā  
  
      Na santi devā iccāhu eke 
 Idheva jivo vibavaṃ upeti  
 Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkatānaṃ 
 Dattu    paññattañca vadanti dānaṃ  
 Tesaṃ vaco arahataṃ saddahāno 
 Tasmā ahaṃ sakuṇe bādhayāmi  
  
   Tuyha   machasaṃ Vi   Datthu   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Cando ca suriyo ca ubho sudassanā 
 Gacchanti obhāsayamantalikkhe  
 Imassa lokassa parassa vā te 
 Kathannu te āhu manussaloke  
  
                    
      Cando ca suriyo ca ubho sudassanā 
 Gacchanti obhāsayamantalikkhe  
 Parassa lokassa na te imassa  
 Devāti te āhu manussaloke  
  
      Ettheva te nihatā hinavādā 
 Ahetukā ye na vadanti kammaṃ  
 Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkatānaṃ 
 Dattu    paññattaṃ ye ca vadanti dānaṃ  
  
      Addhā hi saccaṃ vacanaṃ tavetaṃ 
 Kathaṃ hi dānaṃ aphalaṃ vadeyya  
 Tathā phalaṃ sukatadukkatānaṃ 
 Dattupaññattañca kathaṃ bhaveyyā 
  
      Kathaṃ karo nintikāro kimācaraṃ 
 Kiṃ sevamāno kena tapoguṇena akkhāhi    me morarājetamatthaṃ    
 Yathā ahaṃ no nirayaṃ pateyyaṃ  
  
                    
      Ye keci atthi samaṇā pathavyā    
 Kāsāvavatthā anagāriyā    te  
 Pātova piṇḍāya caranti kāle 
 Vikālacariyā viratā hi santo  
  
      Te tattha kālenupasaṅkamitvā 
 Pucchasi    yante manaso piyaṃ siyā  
 Te te    pavakkhanti yathā pajānaṃ 
 Imassa lokassa parassa catthaṃ  
  
                    
      Tacaṃva jiṇṇaṃ urago purāṇaṃ 
 Paṇḍupalāsaṃ harito dumova  
 Phasappahino mama luddabhāvo 
 Pajahā    mahaṃ luddakabhāvamajja  
  
   Datthu   machasaṃ   Kāsāya vatthā anagāriyaṃ caranti   machasaṃ syā 
   Akkhāhi taṃ dāni   machasaṃ   Puccha hi   machasaṃ 
   Rāja   tama tthaṃ   machasaṃ   Taṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Pathabyā   machasaṃ   Jahā   machasaṃ syā  
  
  
                    
      Ye cāpi me sakuṇā atthi baddhā    
 Satāni nekāni nivesanasmiṃ  
 Tesaṃpahaṃ    jivataṃ ajja dammi 
 Mokkhañca te patto    sakaṃ niketaṃ  
  
                    
      Luddo cari pāsahattho araññe 
 Bādhetuṃ    morādhipatiṃ yasassiṃ 
 Bandhitvā    morādhipatiṃ yasassiṃ 
 Dukkhā pamucci    yathāhaṃ pamuttoti  
   Mahāmorajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Yadesamānā vicarimbha pabbatāni vanāni ca  
 Anvesaṃ vicariṃ    ñāti    teme adhigatā mayā 
  
      Bahuṃ idaṃ    mulaphalaṃ bhakkho cāyaṃ anappako  
 Rammā cimā giri nadiyo phāsu vāso bhavissati  
  
      Idhevāhaṃ vasissāmi saha sabbehi ñātihi  
 Appossukko nirāsaṅki asoko akutobhayo  
  
      Aññaṃ hi lenaṃ     pariyesa santu no idha vijjati  
 So taccha sukare hanti idhāgantvā varaṃ varaṃ 
  
      Konambhākaṃ idha sattu ko ñāti susamāgate  
 Appadhaṃse padhaṃseti tamme akkhātha pucchitā  
                    
      Uddhaggarāji migarājā bali dāṭhāvudho migo  
 So taccha sukare     hanti idhāgantvā varaṃ varaṃ 
  
      Na no dāṭhā na vijjanti balaṃ kāye samuhataṃ     
 Sabbe samagagā hutvāna vasaṃ kāhāma ekakaṃ  
  
      Hadayaṅgamaṃ kaṇṇasukhaṃ vācaṃ bhāsasi tacchata yopi yuddhe palāyetha     
 tampi pacchā hanāmase  
  
   Bandhā   machasaṃ syā   Bahuñcidaṃ   machasaṃ vi 
   Tesaṃ ahaṃ   machasaṃ syā    Najjo   machasaṃ syā  
   Sattā   machasaṃ    Sukaraṃ   vi 
   Bādhetu   machasaṃ syā    Samohataṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Bandhitvā   machasaṃ syā    Palāyeyyu syā palāyetha   machasaṃ 
   Dukkhā pamuñca machasaṃ sapamovi   syā vi  
   Ñātiṃ   machasaṃ vi  
  
                    
                    
      Pāṇātipāti cirato nu ajja 
 Abhayaṃ nu te sabbabhutesu dinanaṃ dāṭhā nu te miga viriyaṃ na santi 
 Yo saṅghapatto kapaṇova jhāyasi  
  
      Na me dāṭhā na vijjanti 
 Balaṃ kāye samuhataṃ  
 Ñāti ca disvāna samaṅgi    ekato 
 Tasmā jhāyāmi vanambhi ekato 
  
      Imassudaṃ yanti disodisaṃ pure 
 Bhayadditā    lenagavesino puthu  
 Tedāni saṅgamma vasanti    ekako 
 Yatthaṭṭhitā duppasahajja te mayā  
  
                    
      Pariṇāyakasampannā sahitā ekavādino    
 Te maṃ samaggā hiṃseyyuṃ tasmā tesaṃ na patthaye    
  
      Ekova indo asure jināti 
 Ekova seno hanti dije pasayha  
 Ekova vyaggho    migasaṅghapatto 
 Varaṃ varaṃ hanti balaṃ hi tādisaṃ  
  
      Naheva indo na seno napi vyaggho migādhipo  
 Samagge sahite ñāti vyagegha    ca kurute vase  
  
      Kumbhilakā sakuṇikā    saṅghino gaṇacārino  
 Sammodamānā ekajjhaṃ uppatanni ḍayanti ca    
  
      Tesaña iyamanānaṃ ekettha apavattati     
 Tañca     seno nitāḷeti veyyagghiyeva sā gati  
  
                    
      Ussāhito jaṭilena     luddenāmisacakkhunā  
 Dāṭhi dāṭhisu pakkhāndi maññamāno yathāpure  
  
                    
      Sādhu sambahulā ñāti api rukkhā araññajā  
 Sukarehi samaggehi vyaggho ekāyane     hato  
  
   Samaggi   machasaṃ vi   Sakuṇikā   machasaṃ syā 
   Bhayaṭṭitā   machasaṃ syā   Damantiva   vi 
   Saranti   vi    Apasakakati   machasaṃ 
   Cāriko   a    Taṃ   vi 
   Nesaṃ apatthave   vi    Jaṭilakena   vi 
   Byaggho   machasaṃ syā    Ekāyyane   machasaṃ 
   Navyagghe syā vyagghona   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Brāhmaṇañceva vyagghañca ubho hanatvāna sukarā  
 Ānandino pamuditā    mahānādañca nādisuṃ  
  
                    
      Tesu    udumbaramulasmiṃ sukarā susamāgatā  
 Tacchakaṃ abhisiñciṃsu tvaṃ no rājāsi issaroti  
   Tacchasukarajātakaṃ  
  
                    
      Vāṇijā samitiṃ katvā nānāraṭṭhato āgatā  
 Dhanāhārā pakkamiṃsu ekaṃ katvāna gāmaṇiṃ  
  
      Te taṃ kantāramāgamma appabhakkhaṃ anodakaṃ  
 Mahānigrodhamaddakkhuṃ sitacchāyaṃ manoramaṃ  
  
      Te ca tattha nisīditvā tassa rukkhassa anodakaṃ  
 Vāṇijā samacintesu bā mohena pārutā  
  
      Addāyate    ayaṃ rukkho api vāri ca    sandati  
 Iṅghassa purimaṃ sākhaṃ mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā  
  
      Sā ca chinnāva pagghari acchaṃ vāriṃ    anāvilaṃ  
 Te tattha nāhātvā ca pivitvā ca yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā  
  
      Dutiyaṃ samacittesu bālā mohena pārutā  
 Iṅghassa dakkhāṇaṃ sākhaṃ mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā 
  
                    
      Sā ca chinnāva pagghari sālimaṃsodanaṃ bahuṃ  
 Appodavaṇṇe kummāse    siṅgiṃ    bidala supiyo  
  
      Te tattha bhutvā khāditvā    yāvaticchaṃsa vāṇijā  
 Tatiyaṃ samacintesuṃ bālā mohena pārutā  
  
      Iṅghassa pacchimaṃ sākhaṃ mayaṃ chindāma vāṇijā  
 Sā ca chintāva paggari nāriyo samalaṅkatā  
  
      Vicitravatthābharaṇā     āmuttatamaṇikuṇḍalā  
 Apisu vāṇijā ekā nāriyo paṇṇavisati  
  
      Samantā parikariṃsu     tassa rukkhassa chādiyā  
 Te tāhi paricā resuṃ     yāvaticciṃsu vāṇijā  
  
   Pamoditā   macasaṃ syā   Pivitvā   vi 
   Te   machasaṃ syā    Vicitta machasaṃ vicitrā   syā 
   Chāyāya   machasaṃ    Parivāriṃsu   machasaṃ 
   Allāyate   machasaṃ syā    Parivāretvā  syā parivāretvā  aṭṭhakathā   Cāriva   
 machasaṃ syā   Kumāse   machasaṃ   Siṅgiveraṃ lasupiyo machasaṃ   siṅgivilada supiyo 
   machasaṃ  
  
                    
      Catutthaṃ samacintesuṃ bālā mohena pārutā 
 Iṅghassa uttaraṃ sākhaṃ chindāma vāṇijā  
  
      Sā ca chinnāva paggari muttā veḷuriye bahu  
 Rajataṃ jātarūpañca kuttiyo paṭiyāni ca  
  
      Kāsikāni ca vatthāni uddiyāne ca kambale    
 Te tattha bhāre bandhitvā yāvaticchiṃsu vāṇijā  
  
      Pañcamaṃ samacintesu bālā mohena pārutā  
 Iṅgassa mulaṃ chindāma api bhiyyo labhāmase  
  
      Athuṭṭhahi satthavāho yācamāno kata ñjalī  
 Nigrodhe kiṃ aparajjhatha    vāṇijā bhaddamatthu te  
  
      Cāridā purimā sākhā annapānaṃ ca dakkhiṇā  
 Nāridā pacchimā sākhā sabbakāme ca attarā 
 Nigrodhe    kiṃ aparajjhatha vāṇijā bhaddamatthu te  
  
      Yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vā  
 Na tassa sākhaṃ bhañjeyya mittadubbho hi    pāpako  
  
      Te ca tassa anāditvā ekassa vacanaṃ bahu  
 Nisitāhi kuṭhārihā mulato taṃ upakkamuṃ  
  
                    
      Tato nāgā nikkhamiṃsu sannaddhā paṇṇavisati  
 Dhanuggahānaṃ tisatā jasahassā ca vammino  
  
                    
      Ete hanatha bhandhatha mā vo muñcittha jīvitaṃ  
 hapetvā satthavāhaṃ sabbe bhasmikarotha te  
  
      Tassā hi paṇḍita poso sampassaṃ atthamattano  
 Lohassa na vasaṃ gacche haneyya    disataṃ manaṃ  
  
      Etamādinavaṃ ñātvā taṇhā dukkhassa sambhavaṃ  
 Vitataṇho anādāno sato bhikkhu paribbajeti  
    Mahāvāṇijajātakaṃ  
  
   Kambalā   machasaṃ sā   Nigrodho kiṃ aparañjati   machasaṃ syā vi 
   Nigrodho  machasaṃ   Vittaduho  machasaṃ   Haneyyārisakaṃ   machasaṃ 
  
                    
                    
      Abbhuto vata lokasmiṃ uppajja lombhaṃsano  
 Dibbo ratho pāturahu vedehassa yasassino  
  
                    
      Devaputto mahiddhiko mātali devasārathi  
 Nimantayittha rājānaṃ vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  
  
      Ehimaṃ rathamāruyha rājaseṭṭha disampati  
 Deva dassanakāmā te tāvatiṃsā saindakā  
  
      Tato ca rājā sādhino pamukho rathamāruhi  
 Sahassayuttaṃ abhiruyha agā devānasantike 
 Taṃ deva paṭinandiṃsu disvā rājānamāgataṃ 
  
      Svāgataṃ te mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ  
 Nisidadāni rājisi devarājassa santike  
  
      Sakkopi paṭinandittha vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  
 Nimantayi ca kāmehati āsanena ca vāsavo  
  
      Sādhu khosi anuppatto āvāsaṃ vasavattinaṃ  
 Vasa devesu rājisi sabbakāmasamiddhisu 
 Tāvatiṃsesu devesu bhuñaṃ kāme amānuse  
  
                    
      Ahaṃ pure saggagato ramāmi 
 Naccehi gitehi ca vāditehi  
 Sodāni ajja na ramāmi sagge 
 Āyuṃ nu khiṇo maraṇaṃ nu sannike 
 Udāhu muḷhosmi janindaseṭṭha  
  
      Navāyu khīṇaṃ maraṇaṃ te dūre nacāpi muḷho naraviriya  seṭṭha  
 Tavañca    puññāni parittakāni 
 Yesaṃ vipākaṃ idha deyittho  
  
      Vasa devānubhāvena rājaseṭṭha disampati  
 Tāvatiṃsesu devesu bhuñja kāme amānuse  
  
   Nāravira   machasaṃ   Taca   machasaṃ  
  
                    
                    
      Yathā yācitakaṃ yānaṃ yathā yācitakaṃ dhanaṃ  
 Evaṃ sampadamevetaṃ yaṃ parato dānapaccayā  
  
      Tacāhametaṃ icchāmi yaṃ parato dānapaccayā  
 Sayaṃ katāni puccāni tamme āveṇikaṃ dhanaṃ  
  
      Sohaṃ gantvā manussesu kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ  
 Dānena samacariyāya saṃyamena damena ca  
 Yaṃ katvā sukino hoti na ca pacchānutappati  
  
      Imāni tāni khettāni imaṃ nikkhaṃ sukuṇḍalaṃ    
 Imā tā bharitā nupā    imā najjo svantiyo  
  
                    
      Imā tā pokkharaṇiyo rammā cakkavākupakujitā  
 Mandālakehi    sañchantā padumuppalakehi ca 
 Yassimā mamāyiṃsu kinnu te disataṃ gatā  
  
      Tānidha    khettāni so bhumibhāgo 
 Te ārāmā te vana me pacārā    
 Tameva mayhaṃ janataṃ apassato 
 Suññāca me nārada khāyate disā  
  
      Diṭṭhā mayā vimānāni obhāsentā    catuddisā  
 Sammukhā devarājassa tidasānañca sammukhā  
  
      Vutthaṃ me bhavanaṃ dibbaṃ    yuttā kāmā amānusā  
 Tāvatiṃsesu devesu tibbakāmasamiddhisu  
  
      Sohaṃ etādisiṃ disvā    puññāyambhi idhāgato  
 Dhammameva carissāmi nāhaṃ rajjena atthiko  
  
                    
      Adaṇḍāvacaraṃ maggaṃ sammābuddadesitaṃ  
 Taṃ maggaṃ paṭipajjissaṃ yena gacchanti subbatiti  
    Sādhinajātakaṃ    
  
   Sakuṇḍalaṃ   machasaṃ syā   Nopā   vi 
   Maṇḍāla   syā   Tānica   machasaṃ 
   Te yeva ārāma vanāni sasañcarā   machasaṃ teyeva ārāma vasupacārā   syā 
   Obāsanataṃ   machasaṃ syā   Dibyaṃ   machasaṃ syā 
   Hitvā   machasaṃ   Sādhina rāja   syā 
  
                    
                    
      Rājā avoca vidhuraṃ    dhamamakāmo yudhiṭṭhilo  
 Buhmaṇe vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me buñejayyuṃ    bhojanaṃ  
 Dakakhiṇaṃ smama dassama yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ 
  
      Dullabhā brāhmaṇā deva silavanto bahussutā  
 Viratā methunā dhamamā ye te bhuññejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
  
      Dasa khalu mahārāja yā tābrāhmaṇajātiyo  
 Tesaṃ vibhaṅgaṃ vicayaṃ vitthārena suṇohi me  
  
      Pasibbake gahetvāna puṇṇe mulassa saṃvute  
 Osadhiyo    ganthenti nahāyanti japanti ca  
  
      Tikicchakasamā rāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā teta mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
                    
      Apetā te buhmaññā     itirājākoravyo  
 Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā 
 Aññepi vidhura pariyesa 
 Silavante bahussute  
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñjeyyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ 
  
      Kiṃkiṇikāyo    gahetvāna ghosenti puratopi te  
 Pesanānipā gaccinti rathacariyāsu sikkhare  
  
      Parivārakasamā rāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
      Apetā te brahmaññā  itirājā koravye   
 Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā 
 Aññe vidhura pariyesa 
 Silavante bahussute  
  
   Viduraṃ   machasaṃ syā   Bhuñejayyu   syā 
   Kāye   machasaṃ syā   Brāhmaññā   syā Brāhma   machasaṃ   Kiṅkaṇikāyo   vi 
 kiṃkiṇiyo   syā  
                    
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahappalaṃ 
  
      Kamaṇḍaluṃ gahetvāna maṃkadaṇḍañca buhmaṇā  
 Paccupessanti rājāno gāmesu nigamesu ca  
 Nādinena vuṭṭhahissāma gamembhi ca vanambhi ca  
  
      Niggāhakasamā rāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase 
      Apetā te buhmaññā     itirājākoravyo  
 Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā 
 Aññepi vidhura pariyesa 
 Silavante bahussute  
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahappalaṃ 
  
      Parūḷhakacca nakhalomā    saṅkadantā rajassirā  
 Okhiṇṇā rajareṇuhi yācakā vicaranti te  
  
      Khāṇughātasamā rāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
                    
      Apetā te buhmaññā     itirājākoravyo  
 Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā 
 Aññepi vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñjeyyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ 
  
      Hariṭakaṃ    āmakaṃ ambaṃ    jambuvibhīṭakaṃ  
 Lakhujaṃ dantapoṇāni kholuvā khadarāni ca  
  
      Rājāyatanaṃ ucchupuṭaṃ dhumanettaṃ madhuañjanaṃ  
 Uccāvacāni paṇiyāni vipaṇenti    janādhipa  
  
      Vāṇijakasamā rāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
      Apetā te brahmaññā  iti rājākoravyo  
 Na te vuccanti brāhmaṇā 
 Aññe vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
  
   Nakhā   machasaṃ   Haritakaṃ   syā   Amkhaṃ jambuṃ vibhedakaṃ   machasaṃ syā   
 Vikkiṇanti   machasaṃ syā  
  
                    
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
  
                    
      Nikkhantabhikkhaṃ    bhuñjanti gāmesveke purohitā  
 Bahu te    paṭipucchanti aṇḍacchedā nilañchakā    
 Pasupi tattha haññanti mahisā sukarā ajā  
  
      Goghātakasamācārā tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
      Apetā te brahmaññā  iti rājā koravyo  
 Na te vuccanti buhmaṇā 
 Aññe vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
  
  
      Asicammaṃ gahetvāna khaggaṃ paggayha brāhmaṇā  
 Vessapathesu tiṭṭhanti satthaṃ abbāhayantipi  
  
      Samā gopanisādehi tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmese  
      Apetā te brahmaññā  iti rājā koravyo  
 Na te vuccanti buhmaṇā 
 Aññe vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
      Araññe kuṭikaṃ katvā kuṭāni kārayanti te  
 Sasakhiḷāre bādhenti āgodhā macchakacchapaṃ  
  
   Nikkhitta bhikkhaṃ   machasaṃ   Bahuṃte   machasaṃ   Aṇḍacechadāni   machasaṃ 
  
                     
      Luddakā te mahārāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇa  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
      Apetā te brahmaññā  iti rājā koravyo  
 Na te vuccanti buhmaṇā 
 Aññe vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
  
                    
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
  
      Aññe dhanassa kāmāhi heṭṭhāmañce pasakkhitā  
 Rājāno upari nabhāyanti somayāge upaṭṭhite  
  
      Malamajjakasamā rāja tepi vuccanti brāhmaṇā  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
      Apetā te brahmaññā  iti rājā koravyo  
 Na te vuccanti buhmaṇā 
 Aññe vidhura pariyesa silavante bahussute  
  
      Virate methunā dhammā ye me bhuñejayyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
 Dakkhiṇaṃ samma dassāma yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
  
                    
      Atthi brāhmaṇā deva silavanto bahussutā  
 Viratā methunā dhammā ye te bhuñjeyyuṃ bhojanaṃ  
  
      Ekañca bhattaṃ bhuñjanti na ca majjaṃ pivanti te  
 Akkhātā te mahārāja tādise nipatāmase  
  
      Ete kho brāhmaṇā vidhura silavanto bahussutā  
 Ete vidhura pariyesa kippañca te nimantayāti  
    Dasabrāhmaṇajātakaṃ  
  
                     
                    
  
      Sukhumālarūpaṃ disvāna    raṭṭhā vivanamāgataṃ  
 Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ mahāsayanamupāsitaṃ   
  
      Tassa te pemakenāhaṃ adāsiṃ baddha    modanaṃ  
 Sālinaṃ vicitaṃ bhattaṃ suciṃ maṃsūpasecanaṃ  
  
      Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha brāhmaṇassa apāpayi    
 Attānaṃ anasitvāna koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te  
  
      Ācariyo brāhmaṇo mayhaṃ kiccākiccesu vyāvaṭo  
 Garu ca āmantaniyo dātumarahāmi bhonaṃ  
  
      Brāhmaṇandāni pucchāmi gotamaṃ rājapujitaṃ  
 Rājā te bhattaṃ pādāsi suciṃ maṃsupasecanaṃ  
  
      Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha isissa bhojanaṃ adā  
 Akhentaññusi dānassa koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te  
  
      Bharāmi putte dāre ca gharesu gathito ahaṃ  
 Bhuñje mānusake kāme anusāsāmi rājino  
  
      Āraññakassa isino cirarattaṃ tapassino  
 Vaddhassa    bhāvitattassa dātumarahāmi bhojanaṃ  
  
      Isiñcadāni pucchāmi kisaṃ dhamanisatthataṃ  
 Parūḷhakacchanakhalomaṃ paṅkadantaṃ rajassiraṃ  
  
      Eko araññe viharasi    nāvakaṅkhasi jivataṃ  
 Bhikkhu kena tayā seyyo yassa tvaṃ bhojanaṃ adā 
  
      Khaṇantālu    kalambāni khīḷālitakkaḷāni ca  
 Dhunaṃ sāmākanivāraṃ saṅghāriyaṃ    pasāriyaṃ  
  
   Disvā   machasaṃ   Mupāvitaiṃ   machasaṃ 
   Vaḍḍha   machasaṃ   Adāsayi   machasaṃ 
   Vuḍḍhassa syā vuḍassa machasaṃ   Vihāsi   machasaṃ 
   Khaṇamāluka   machasaṃ   Sāriyaṃ  machasaṃ sa saṃhāriya pahāriyaṃ   syā 
  
                    
  
      Sākaṃ bhisaṃ madhuṃ maṃsaṃ padarāmalakāni ca  
 Tāni āhatva    bhuñjāmi atthi me so pariggabho  
  
                    
      Pacanto apacantassa amamasasa akiñcano  
 Anādānassa sādāno dātumarahāmi bhojanaṃ  
      Bhikkhuñcadāni pucchāmi tuṇhimāsina subbataṃ  
 Isi te bhantaṃ pādāsi suciṃ maṃsupasecanaṃ  
  
      Taṃ tvaṃ bhattaṃ paṭiggayha tuṇhi bhuñjasi ekako  
 Nāññaṃ kañci nimantesi koyaṃ dhammo namatthu te  
  
      Na pacāmi na pācemi na chindāmi na chedaye  
 Taṃ maṃ akikañcanaṃ ñatvā sabbapāpehi ārataṃ  
  
      Cāmenana bhikkhamādāya akkhiṇena kamaṇḍaluṃ  
 Isi me bhattaṃ pādāsi suciṃ maṃsupasecanaṃ  
  
      Ete hi dātumarahanti samamā sapariggahā  
 Paccaṇikamahaṃ maññe yo dātāraṃ nimantaye  
  
                    
      Atthāya vata me ajja idhāgañji    rathesabho  
 Ito pubbe na pajānāmi    yattha dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ  
  
      Raṭṭhesu giddhā rājāno kiccākiccesu brāhmaṇā  
 Isi mulaphale giddhā vippamuttā ca bhikkhavoti  
    Bhikkhāparamparajātakaṃ  
  
                    
  
 Pakiṇaṇakanipātaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ 
  
 Tassuddānaṃ  
 Suva kinnaramukkakharājina so  
 Bhisajāta mahesi kapotavaro  
 Atha mora satacchaka vāṇijako 
 Atha rāja dasabrāhmaṇā bhikkhaparanti  
  
   Āharitvā   vi machasaṃ   Idhāgacchi vi machasaṃ   Sohaṃ ajja pajānāmi   machasaṃ
